Changing Bureaus to Sections: The various bureaus of the city government are now being changed to sections. A public notice has been issued stating: "It has been found that the city government's revenue from all municipal expenses is significantly less than the expenditure each year. Unless measures are taken to rectify the situation, and to separately reduce and merge departments, it will be difficult to achieve a balance between income and expenditure. It has also been decided to comply with the government's orders to reduce the scope of operations and change the bureaus to sections, in order to prevent waste and eliminate redundancy. From the 16th of this month, all bureaus except for the Public Security Bureau will be abolished immediately. All assistant officials should be dismissed immediately. If there are any incomplete procedures in hand, they must be quickly cleared up and handed over to the newly appointed personnel."

Siam Restricts Chinese Immigrants 68

(Continued from the 16th)

(Article 11) When inspecting ships entering Siam, if the inspecting officer believes that any foreigner on board belongs to any of the prohibited categories under any article of this law, he may order the foreigner to be sent back on the original ship. If this is difficult, he may detain the foreigner and send him back on another ship as soon as possible. If the aforementioned foreigner needs to be investigated, he may be detained on the ship or at other convenient locations during the investigation period. The cost of sending and detaining the foreigner shall be borne by the shipowner or charterer. At any time, or from any vehicle coming to Siam, if the number of foreigners is too large, causing excessive time and expense for detention, inspection, or obtaining certificates, the inspecting officer may, after recording, issue a temporary permit to any foreigner, allowing him to enter Siam. The foreigner must personally go to the inspecting officer at the time and place specified on the permit for inspection or to obtain a certificate. (Article 12) The inspecting officer may detain and investigate any foreigner coming to Siam after this law comes into effect if he suspects that he is on the prohibited list. If it is confirmed that he should be deported, he shall be expelled from the country. (Article 13) If the shipowner fails to comply with the provisions of Article 5, he shall be fined up to 400 Siamese Baht. (Article 14) Any foreigner entering Siam who conceals his identity or name with the intention of evading the provisions of this law or violates the orders of the inspecting officer shall be fined up to 1,000 Siamese Baht. (Article 15) Anyone who intentionally brings in a foreigner in violation of this law or helps a foreigner evade this law shall be sentenced to imprisonment for up to six months, or a fine of up to 200 Siamese Baht, or both. (Article 16) The order of the inspecting officer prohibiting a foreigner from entering Siam must be notified to the foreigner in writing. He may appeal within 48 hours to the minister for a decision, which shall be final. Anyone who does not admit that he is a foreigner may request a court decision. (Article 17) Anyone detained for investigation by an inspecting officer enforcing this law shall not be detained for more than four days. However, a detention order issued by the court shall be valid for ten days from the date of issuance. If necessary, the detention order may be renewed upon the request of the inspecting officer. (Article 18) The Minister of Interior is responsible for the administration and enforcement of this law, and therefore has the power to issue ministerial regulations for its implementation. These regulations shall come into effect upon publication in the Government Gazette. Promulgated on July 11th, 2470 BE (Buddhist Era), the third year of the current King of Siam's reign. (End)

New Investigation into Japanese Management of Yanbian 69

Jilin Correspondence: The Japanese have long coveted the land of my Yanbian region. Their aggression in the four counties of Yanji, Hunchun, Wangqing, and Helong is mainly carried out through three instruments: police, education, and economy. The current situation is investigated as follows: (1) Police: The Japanese, taking advantage of the privilege of extraterritoriality, arbitrarily summon, interrogate, and arrest Koreans and垦民in the four counties. Although the Sino-Japanese Tumen River Treaty of the past stipulated that each consulate was only allowed one police officer to handle cases, with their inching-forward policy and the method of using police to replace troops in the Hunchun Incident, the number has increased to more than 800 today, distributed in 18 police stations. Japanese police stations are established wherever transportation is convenient and the population is dense. There are 18 places including Longjing Village, Juzi Street, Toudaogou, Wangqing, Hunchun, Liangshui Quanzi, Heidongzi, Gaya River, Yilan, Goujie, Mandong, Nanyangping, Helong, Budong, Erdaogou, Tongfosi, Tianbaoshan, and Badaogou. In addition to setting up Japanese police, Korean Residents Associations are also established in each place to supplement the insufficient strength of the Japanese police. The Police Headquarters is located in Longjing Village, and the other 17 branch offices are directly managed and commanded by the headquarters.

(2) Education: In terms of the number of schools, Japanese education in Yanbian is not as numerous as those established by the Chinese. However, in terms of funding, the funding for Chinese education in the four counties is less than two-fifths of theirs. The following is a description of Japanese education: (1) Gando Central School, located in Longjing Village, has more than 800 students. It is run by the Korean Governor-General and specializes in teaching the children of Koreans. (2) Ordinary Schools, located in Juzi Street, Toudaogou, Baicaogou, and Hunchun, each have one school. They are also run by the Korean Governor-General and are specifically established to teach Korean children. (3) Gando Normal Higher Elementary School, located in Longjing Village, is run by the Korean Governor-General, but it is a school designated by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and specializes in enrolling Japanese children. There are currently more than 130 students. (4) Schools run by the Guangming Society: 1. Yongxin Middle School with attached Normal and Elementary Departments; 2. Guangming Higher Girls' School; 3. Guangming Girls' School; 4. Guangming Kindergarten. The above schools are all located in Longjing Village and are run by the Japanese, Hidaka Heiji郎, who raises funds in his private capacity and receives subsidies from the Korean Governor-General. They specialize in educating Korean children and have a total of more than 650 students. In addition, there are also Japanese-subsidized Korean study halls (i.e., private schools for Koreans, subsidized by the Japanese, using Japanese textbooks). There are more than 50 of these in the four counties of Yanbian. Currently, our side is trying to recover education, but the Japanese have decided to oppose it. Therefore, judging from the current situation, I am afraid it will be very difficult to do so.

(3) Economy: Economic aggression is the sole policy of modern imperialism to invade other countries. The Japanese want to buy up all the land in my four counties of Yanbian, so they have established the following economic institutions throughout the four counties: (1) Joseon Bank Longjing Village Branch; (2) Oriental Development Company Gando Branch; (3) Gando Trust Company; (4) Gando Development Company; (5) Gando Financial Department. The above companies are all located in Longjing Village and specialize in handling banking deposit and loan matters. The interest rate is lower than the average, averaging 1.2% per month. Real estate and grains must be used as collateral. Currently, 3/5ths of the Koreans and Chinese people in the four counties, tempted by the low interest rates, have had their collaterals confiscated. In addition, there is also a Financial Department, nominally an economic institution to help Korean farmers, in each of Jiaozijie, Toudaogou, and Hunchun, specifically to absorb Korean land. According to the investigation, 4/5ths of the Korean land has been absorbed by the Financial Department. This year, the Japanese, in order to make a sharp advance, have further reduced the interest rate, so the general Chinese and Korean people are suffering from economic pressure and have no choice but to disregard the future and willingly suffer the consequences. I hope that our officials and people will pay attention to this.

News Trend in Harbin 70

Xue Dake runs the Donghua News to Insult Colleagues. Harbin Correspondence: After Zhang Jingxian came to the Changchun Special Zone, he adopted a policy of suppressing public opinion on the suggestion of Guan Hongyi, the president of the Harbin Public News. Those that have been registered have their freedom of speech restricted, and those who apply for registration are generally not approved. As a result, the special zone's news industry has been extremely dull for the past two years. The authorities believe that opening one less newspaper can save them one less trouble. Guan Hongyi, who made the suggestion to the government, has his own ulterior motives. Because Guan runs a Chinese-Russian Public News, which has made considerable profits over the years, he believes that if this continues, there will be fewer competitors and the profits can continue unabated. This suggestion happened to be deeply in line with the authorities' wishes and became an ironclad case, an unbreakable precedent in the special zone. Last autumn, Xue Dake (Zi Qi), who previously founded the Yellow News in Beiping, came to Harbin to run a Donghua Daily. Because it was not allowed to be registered in the special zone, he first obtained a permit in the Jilin jurisdiction outside Daowai and issued it for nearly a year. Recently, relying on his clever maneuvering, he actually obtained a permit from the special zone and was allowed to register, and the Russian version was also approved for registration at the same time. Xue then moved his newspaper to Daoli. Since its publication, the Chinese version has not developed much, but the Russian version's sales have been increasing rapidly. Guan Hongyi, who runs the Russian Public News, is quite jealous. He has successively destroyed Xue's copyright in the special zone and Liaoning, but to no avail. At this time, the Lubu News and the Aurora News, which are run by the Russian White Party in Harbin, were also affected by the Donghua Daily's sales, so they secretly formed a joint venture with the Russian Public News and vigorously attacked the Russian Donghua Daily. They also bribed the Chinese tabloid Noon News to attack the Chinese Donghua News in the name of the Newspaper Industry Association and revealed Xue's history as one of the Thirteen Taibao of the Hongxian Imperial Restoration. Although the Harbin Newspaper Industry Association exists in name, several newspapers such as the International Cooperative News have not joined the association. Therefore, when this matter first arose, the newspapers that had not joined the association did not pay much attention to it. Later, Xue Dake was scolded too harshly, and a month ago, he wrote a communication that resembled an editorial but was not, and published it on the Chinese version, which contained "For example, when a person walks in a dog country, the dog barks at the person, and the person can only scold it away, and must never imitate the dog's voice and bark back." In addition, the language also invaded the International Cooperative News, Chenguang News, and Dongsan Province Business News, discussing the personality of journalists, etc. This aroused public indignation, and the newspapers convened a meeting and unanimously decided to issue a general attack order against the Donghua News. At least each newspaper would attack the Donghua News for a week. Xue Dake initially resisted, then became silent, and finally asked someone to mediate with the newspapers. The newspapers put forward two conditions: first, the Donghua Daily must publish an apology to the newspapers; second, it must suspend publication for a week. Xue agreed to the first condition, but refused the second condition because it would affect the newspaper's business. The mediation lasted for two weeks, but ultimately to no avail. The newspapers then began to attack again. Xue then mobilized Zhang Jinghui to instruct Bao Wenbo, the chief of the Special Police Department, to invite the chief writers of the newspapers and order them to cease fire. Bao notified the newspapers on the 18th of this month, and his tone contained an order. The newspapers believed that this attack on the Donghua News was merely a debate about the personality of journalists, and did not violate local laws, so the authorities should not forcibly interfere. Therefore, no one went that day. The trend is still unresolved. (August 20th)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 71

Reactionary Criminal to be Transferred to the Garrison Headquarters: Zhang Yiming, a teacher at Chun Shen Elementary School in the city, was arrested by the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau inside Caoqiao City Elementary School along with Ge Naibin due to suspicion of reactionary activities. They were handed over to the High Court. After investigation by Prosecutor Jin Henian, a public prosecution was filed. The court was originally scheduled to open a trial this morning (27th). However, because the Public Security Bureau had submitted a proposal to the provincial government for approval, the provincial government issued instructions the day before yesterday, ordering Zhang Yiming to be transferred to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for review. After receiving the order, Director Zou ordered two policemen to prepare documents and go to the High Court to retrieve Zhang Yiming and transfer him to the Garrison Headquarters for review yesterday morning. The trial originally scheduled by the High Court for today must be postponed.

The Unexplained Death Case is Judged by the Local Court: In the case of the unexplained death of Han Jinshi in Gejia Lane, Chuangmen, her relatives, Han Guoduo and Han Guolin, reported it. The Local Court ruled that Han Guoduo and Han Guolin were each sentenced to three years imprisonment for false accusation and fraud, and each fined 500 yuan. The Han Guoduo brothers were dissatisfied with the ruling and appealed to the High Court. Yesterday morning (26th), Lin Dawen, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division One, came to court to announce the verdict. The original verdict against Han Guoduo and Han Guolin was revoked. Han Guoduo and Han Guolin were each sentenced to one year and eight months imprisonment for fraud, and each fined 100 yuan. Han Guoduo and others declared in court that they were dissatisfied with the verdict and would appeal to the Supreme Court.

The Water Police Team Arrests Lake Bandits: The First Detachment and the Second Guerrilla Detachment of the 14th Water Public Security Team arrested Li Changyin, the "Little Boss" of the No. 10 bandit boat of the Taihu Guerrilla Team, and two accomplices, Lü Kuzi, at the Shanghai Wheel Terminal in Zhenpiao Town. Three rifles were also seized. They were escorted to Suzhou yesterday (26th). According to their confessions, bandit leaders Zhong Zhaokui and Zhou Asi ordered them to regroup at Taipu Pier in Taihu before the tenth day of the seventh lunar month. Director Gong has already telegraphed his subordinates to take strict precautions based on the confessions.

Songjiang 72

Robbery and Kidnapping Case at Desheng Port: At Xujiage, about three li east of Huayang Bridge in the eastern suburbs of the city, near Desheng Port on the Huangpu River, where boats come and go day and night, it was reported that at around 11 o'clock last night (the 25th), more than 30 armed robbers speaking in a local dialect broke through the back door of Xu Wenjie's house and rushed in. The homeowner was unable to escape and was immediately threatened into silence, allowing the robbers to plunder at will. After three hours, they only found 50 yuan in cash, several gold rings, and clothing. Believing they were being deceived, the robbers burned the homeowner and his wife. Before leaving, they forced Xu Wenjie onto a boat. His nine-year-old son, Cui Guan, and ten-year-old nephew, Huanzhang, witnessing the scene, cried out in terror, so the two children were also kidnapped. The robbers then searched the house of Xu Da, a cousin living nearby, but he had already been alerted and led his family to jump over the wall and escape, avoiding harm. After the incident, the robbers boarded two boats and headed towards Panlongtang. After receiving the report, the county government ordered a thorough investigation and also notified the first water police team to investigate.

Arrest of Absconding Section Chief: The Finance Department previously ordered the county government to arrest Quan Weinong, the former chief of the General Affairs Section of the Nanhui County Finance Bureau. The administrative police chief, Dong Futang, was dispatched and has apprehended and handed him over to the county. It is said that he absconded with funds, prompting the arrest order. He has been temporarily detained by the county government in the detention center, pending a report to the provincial authorities for further instructions.

Qingpu 73

Bandits Appear on the Border: The towns of Jinze, Xicen, Anzhuang, etc., under the jurisdiction of the county, are located on the edge of the Dianshan Lake, close to Xitang Town in Zhejiang Province. Yesterday (the 24th), a large group of bandit ships and bandits were seen circling around Jinze and Xicen. A small steamship traveling from Songjiang through Qingpu Zhujie Pavilion to Jinze suddenly turned back to Zhujie Pavilion midway, causing widespread panic. Later, the water police team was dispatched to pursue them, but the bandits, hearing the news, fled towards Dianshan Lake.

Former Ninth District Chief Accused: Dai Junxuan, the former Ninth District Chief of the county, was ordered by the department to go to the province for training due to poor performance. Wang Daohang was appointed as his replacement. It is now reported that after Dai handed over his duties, people from the district, such as Ma Hai, accused Dai of financial irregularities and lack of transparency during his tenure as district chief. They have compiled the facts and filed a complaint with the local government.

Jiangyin 74

Meeting to Solicit Tobacco Treasury Bonds: The county government convened a meeting of district chiefs on the 25th to discuss the solicitation of tobacco treasury bonds. It was decided that the solicitation would be conducted separately in urban and rural areas. The urban area was tasked with raising 6,800 yuan, and the rural area with 13,200 yuan. There are eight level C districts and five level D districts. Each level C district is to raise 1,200 yuan, and each level D district is to raise 880 yuan. The five or six level C districts are to each raise 500 yuan. The remaining 1,400 yuan from all level C districts will be covered by adding 100 yuan to each level C district, and 800 yuan to the urban area. The receipts for the treasury bonds should be issued by the Finance Bureau. The deadline for each district to submit their contributions is the end of this month, with the first 30% due first, and the remaining 20% due by September 10th.

Fundraising for Important Public Security Meeting: Due to the importance of public security and the high costs involved, the county government held a meeting the other day. The Chamber of Commerce then convened a meeting of various industries and decided that each district office should raise 1,000 yuan, and each industry and money shop should raise 2,000 yuan, to be used for this purpose. Yesterday, Yin Zhongren sent letters to solicit contributions.

Huzhou 75

Escorted Thief Escapes by Swimming: The Wuxing County Public Security Bureau extracted four thieves from the prison the other day, and dispatched police officers Chen Jinrong and others to escort them to the Anji County government for prosecution. The police officers then escorted the criminals on the Meixi steamship. Unexpectedly, in the middle of the journey, one of the bandits broke the iron chain and jumped into the river. Because the police officers were not good swimmers, they allowed him to escape by swimming. Yesterday, the police officers returned to the bureau and reported the circumstances of the escape.

Administrative Inspectors Come to Huzhou for Investigation: In order to investigate the administrative conditions of various counties in the province, the Civil Affairs Department of this province has specially dispatched 11 inspectors, including Zhang Mengqi, to inspect the administrative conditions of various counties in different regions. It is now known that the inspector for the counties under the jurisdiction of Huzhou is Zheng Yu, who is expected to come to Huzhou for inspection soon.

Wuxi 76

The Silkworm Seed Case Has Been Resolved: The Silkworm Industry Enforcement Office of the Agricultural and Mining Department stationed in Wuxi recently seized a large batch of autumn silkworm seeds produced by various seed production sites that had not been approved for registration, such as the Huicheng Silkworm Breeding and Seed Production Site. They were sent to the Xiyu Cold Storage in Guangqin District for storage. The matter was reported to the Agricultural and Mining Department for instructions. The evening before last, hundreds of villagers, claiming to be buyers, flocked to the Enforcement Office to request the return of the seeds, causing a great disturbance. It is now known that Yi Jianding, the deputy director of the Enforcement Office, together with personnel dispatched by the Public Security Bureau, went to the front of the Xiyu Cold Storage in Guangqin District at 9:00 a.m. yesterday and returned the substandard seeds that had been confiscated in their entirety. In addition to returning the silkworm seeds to the silkworm farmers, the seed prices collected by the seed production sites from the silkworm farmers must be returned. The county government should be requested to order the heads of each site to return the money to the silkworm farmers. The heads of each site should be held responsible for the illegal acts and should be punished with a fine of up to 80% according to the penalty regulations of the Agricultural Products Inspection Office issued by the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining. It is reported that the substandard seeds confiscated in the cold storage include 2,591 sheets from the Huinong Silkworm Breeding and Seed Production Site, 1,112 sheets from the Wuxi Zhaofeng Seed Production Site (Minyi Branch), and 8,861 sheets from the Jingjiang Jijiang Seed Production Site. However, there are rumors that certain officials of the Enforcement Office were privately negotiating to return the confiscated substandard silkworm seeds from a certain seed production site in exchange for 600 yuan. After Yi, the deputy director, learned of this, he launched a thorough investigation because it concerned the reputation of the entire Enforcement Office, determined to uncover the truth.

Appeal for Increased Pig Tax: Last year, the Construction Department of Jiangsu Province instructed the county government of this county to order each meat dealer to add a special construction tax of one dime per pig. After repeated appeals from the meat merchants, the result was a reduction of five cents per pig. Recently, Jiang Hongzhang, a standing committee member of the Wuxi Meat Industry Association, presented a petition to the provincial government, stating that the Construction Department was disregarding the difficulties of the merchants and that the implementation of this harsh tax was unbearable for the merchants. He requested that the provincial government order the tax to be abolished. After receiving the petition, Chairman Ye of the provincial government ruled that the appeal was illegal and should be rejected. However, if the people had difficulties, they could still submit a petition to the Construction Department.

Murder Case in Taibo Market: A villager from Taibo Market in the county was somehow beaten to death the other day and his body was abandoned at the intersection of the Gebei Township Hai Da Tomb Road in the market. Yesterday, the county government sent people by boat to the countryside to perform an autopsy according to the law. It was also reported that the deceased's upper body was naked, he was about 30 years old, and there was a blue cloth short shirt beside him, containing a live hen. Whether he was a chicken thief who was beaten to death and abandoned there or whether someone deliberately set up a false impression is unknown.

Changzhou 77

Bandit Zhang Yinggen Captured in Baojiatang: Bandits frequently appeared in Laogu Bridge in the fourth district of Wuyi County, and cases of vendetta killings and kidnappings were often heard. Recently, bandit traces were also discovered in villages near Anjia She. Zhang Zhufang, a patrol officer of the first sub-station of the fourth public security bureau, together with the chamber of commerce, learned that Zhang Yinggen of Baojiatang in that area was an accomplice of the bandit Bao Genfu, who had been killed in Laogu Bridge. On the 24th, they went and arrested him and escorted him to the sub-station. On the 25th, they prepared a document and sent him to the county for interrogation.

County Government Interrogates Accumulated Bandit Zou Pigen: Liu Yuanshan, the leader of the second platoon of the first company of the police team stationed in Xixiashu, Wuyi County, recently captured the accumulated bandit Zou Pigen and sent the criminal to the brigade headquarters. On the 25th, he was sent to the county for interrogation. The criminal directly admitted to robbing six times in the vicinity of Yangqiao and Liuweigang, killing a detective, and receiving a lot of stolen money. After the interrogation, he was ordered to be detained pending further action.

Zhenjiang 78

Chamber of Commerce Entrusts Hu and Lu to Take Office: The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce was reorganized, and Lu Xiaobo was elected as chairman, and Hu Jianchun and others were elected as standing committee members. The second meeting was held yesterday. The temporary chairman Yu Xiaochuan reported that Lu had sent a letter stating that he would accept the position of executive committee member but would not take the position of chairman. Hu also sent a letter stating that he would accept the position of executive committee member but would not continue to serve as standing committee member. District Chief Training Class Begins: The Civil Affairs Department believed that the poor performance of the district chiefs was due to insufficient education, and had ordered all counties to send the district chiefs to the province for training. However, due to matters such as the handover of duties by the district chiefs, the arrangements could not be completed in time, and the deadline was extended to this month. Currently, students from various counties have registered one after another, and classes began yesterday. Zhai Yifu, the education director of the training class, gave a speech to the students, explaining in detail the significance of Director Hu's decision to recall the district chiefs from various counties for training.

Bandit News Thirty Li from the City: On the afternoon of the 24th of this month, more than 100 bandits, all armed, arrived at the Wujin Baojia area in the fourth map of the fourteenth capital of the second district, thirty li outside the city, that is, the area west of Changshan Mountain, Yaohua Mountain, and Chejiabian. They demanded 1,000 yuan, threatening to burn houses and kill people if their demands were not met. They also tied up Wang, who agreed to pay 500 yuan, but had no cash on hand and would have to wait until the rice was sold. The bandits refused and gave him five days to pay. Wang has now sent someone to the city to find a way to raise the money.

Gaoyou 79

Salt Tai Ban Nanyu Steamer Robbed: The Salt Tai Ban Nanyu small steamer of the Dasheng Company was sailing to the Caohan Village in Dongtai County at about 12 o'clock the other night, when it suddenly encountered many bandits. The bandits, fearing that there were soldiers and police escorting the ship, shouted for the crew to surrender their weapons. Then they fired more than a dozen shots as a warning. The captain of the ship, fearing that the passengers would be injured by the bullets, stopped the ship. The bandits swarmed onto the ship and, directed by a child of about ten years old, conducted a thorough search. None of the passengers were spared. The loss is estimated to be more than 10,000 yuan.

Sun Jinzhang for the Disabled Hospital and the School for the Blind and Deaf,

Bandits from Tong, Ru, and Hai Counties Surrender: Eight or nine hundred bandits from the counties of Tong, Ru, and Hai have surrendered to Liu Zuhan, the Commander of the Jiangbei Guerrilla Forces, through Cao Kuijiu. Qingjiang 81

Bandits Attack and Break Through Yugou Town: It is reported that several hundred bandits from Siyang County passed through Zhuangwei in the county and ate dinner at Sankeshu Market in Huaiyin. At night, they went straight to Yugou Town, which is twelve li from Sankeshu, and attacked from the northwest, south, and three sides. At that time, more than ten county police officers in the town, together with the merchants, came out to fight the enemy from all sides. The two sides held each other until about 4:00 a.m. today (the 22nd). Finally, due to the disparity in numbers, the police team, led by service member Zhang Hongxing, withdrew to Dingji. Dozens of merchants and civilians defending the town also carried their guns and fled from the east gate and the small north gate of Yugou. The bandits then waded into the water from the south moat and climbed in. They then entered through the west and north gates and burned and looted at will. The merchants and civilians in the town also supported the old and carried the young, fleeing in groups to Jiangjiawa and Dingjiaji in the east of the town. Commander Huang of the 266th Regiment, upon hearing the news, sent a company of soldiers and two cannons. Magistrate Xu also urgently sent people to report to Zhao Zhenhua, the deputy captain of the police brigade, who rushed back from Nanxinji to Langshi Town, south of Yugou, and joined forces with the officers and soldiers of the 266th Regiment, beginning to attack the south gate of Yugou. At the same time, the two merchants from the west Yun'an also telegraphed Hu Xingchi, the Deputy Director of Transportation and the Chief of Anti-Smuggling Bureau of Huaibei, requesting troops. However, according to those who fled from the town, the bandits, after breaking through the town, hated the resistance of the merchants and civilians, and carried out a massacre. They also set fires everywhere, and the light shone twenty miles away, a great catastrophe that had never been seen before.

Huaiyin Negotiates Rice Purchases in Gaoyou: Previously, merchants from Huaiyin purchased dozens of dan of rice in Shangyou. On the 11th of this month, dozens of poor people from Gaoyou prevented the rice from being loaded onto the ship for transportation to Huaiyin and arbitrarily poured river water on it, making it difficult to sustain. Upon receiving the news, the Huaiyin rice merchants joined forces and went to see Xu Jiaqing, the county magistrate, asking him to maintain the food supply of Huaiyin. Xu telegraphed the Civil Affairs Department of the provincial government, requesting them to telegraph Magistrate Wang of Gaoyou to release the rice. On the one hand, Huang Zihou, the chairman of the Huaiyin Rice Industry Association, also submitted a report to the Gaoyou County government, requesting that they abide by the provincial order, allow the free flow of rice in the province, and inform the people of Gaoyou that they must not block the rice in the future. It is now known that Magistrate Xu has received a reply from the provincial government, stating that they have telegraphed the Magistrate of Gaoyou and ordered him to release the rice.

Hangzhou 82

Financial Difficulties: The finances of Zhejiang Province are extremely strained, and income is not sufficient to cover expenses. The province is in debt of more than 10 million yuan, with a monthly income of only 600,000 to 700,000 yuan, while expenses are more than 1 million yuan. The province relies entirely on borrowing to maintain its operations, which is extremely dangerous. The Finance Department is actively seeking ways to increase revenue in order to fundamentally alleviate the situation. After the establishment of the Provincial Economic Committee, the accounting system will be strictly defined, and efforts will be made to reorganize the finances.

Officials Sent Abroad to Study Agricultural Affairs: The Zhejiang Province has already conducted examinations and selected students for government-funded study abroad programs. The Construction Department has specially requested the provincial government to allow Zhao Cai, the current county magistrate of Wukang County and one of the students selected for study abroad, to also be responsible for studying agricultural affairs, giving him the title of inspector and subsidizing him with 200 yuan per month for inspection expenses. The proposal has already been approved.

County Public Security Bureau Chief Accused: On the 13th and 14th of June, the Jiaxing County Public Security Bureau violated orders and conscripted laborers. Various legal groups telegraphed General Commander Chiang Kai-shek for relief. The telegram replied that the Zhejiang Provincial Government had been ordered to investigate. Subsequently, the Zhejiang authorities, based on the petition of 200 merchants in Hecheng, ordered the Civil Affairs Department to investigate. At the beginning of this month, Xu Ajin, who was conscripted as a laborer, complained to the Jiaxing Local Court that Fang Zhuangyou, the secretary of the county government, Mo Lanxun, the chief of the County Public Security Bureau, and Qiu Zeshen, the chief of the second sub-bureau, had obstructed his freedom of movement. He stated that the pain he suffered from being forcibly taken away by the police was unbearable, and that his family of several people had no means of living. The Jiaxing Sub-Court requested instructions from the High Court on jurisdiction, which was approved and transferred to the Hangzhou County Court for trial. Now that the High Court has transferred the case file to the Hangzhou Court, the trial has been scheduled for the morning of the 28th.

Pinghu 84

Hunan Refugees Rob and Borrow Silver and Rice: Three hundred and some Hunan refugees arrived in Zhapu the other day. Director Duanmu of the Public Security Bureau ordered them to temporarily stay in the City God Temple and sent police to monitor them. More than 30 yuan was raised for them and given to their leaders, Liu Yuxiang and Tang Yanhai, with instructions to leave Zhapu. Unexpectedly, when they were about to depart, about a hundred of them went to Zhang Chuchen's house in the east city and surrounded it, demanding property. The Zhang family was extremely frightened. The Director of the Public Security Bureau, upon hearing the news, rushed with the patrol police to suppress them. As a result, they took away five shi of white rice and 20 yuan before leaving with shouts.

New County Magistrate Arrives in Pinghu: The county government received a phone call last night, stating that the newly appointed County Magistrate Shen will take the early train to He today (the 25th) and then transfer to a boat to Pinghu, arriving at the county government tomorrow to take over his duties.

Kidnapping Case in Chaonitan: The bandit leaders Taibao Ashu and Wang Ajiu sent threatening letters to the Xu families in Chaonitan, demanding 5,000 yuan, which they did not receive. Ningbo 85

Team Member Tragically Killed by Bandits: Lin Yutang, a team member of the joint military and police investigation office in this city, was ordered on the 23rd to lead troops to the vicinity of Hongtang in Cixi to round up bandits. Because it was midnight, the team member and the soldiers dispersed sentries at the train station there. After some time, a bandit slowly approached. Lin shouted, "Who is there?" The bandit acted suspicious and fled. At that time, Lin was afraid that he was a villager, so he did not shoot, but closely pursued the bandit. Seeing that he was being chased very closely, the thief fired two shots from a pistol. Lin then realized that he was indeed a bandit. Because it was dark, he could not aim, so he used a flashlight to illuminate the bandit. Unexpectedly, the bandit was very alert and, taking advantage of the flashlight, shot at the light, hitting the team member in the abdomen. He was wounded and fell to the ground. The soldiers behind him, seeing that he was injured, carried him to the train station and temporarily settled him there. At the same time, they divided up and chased the bandits. As a result, two bandits were captured and sent to the investigation office for interrogation. Team member Lin died soon after due to his serious injuries. It is reported that the bandit suppression command is planning to provide generous compensation and condolences to the family of the team member, who was killed in the line of duty, in order to comfort the loyal soul.

Two Train Stations to Be Rebuilt Soon: The train stations in this city are temporary in nature, so the station buildings are simple. Now, because business is good, the platforms are too short, and the offices are insufficient, it has been decided to build permanent train stations to facilitate operations. It is also planned to build an overpass over the tracks and move the station gate to the opposite side of the railway garden. Drawings are being rushed, and the construction period should not be far off.

Elementary School Student Injured While Peeping at Movies: Shi Afang, a 14-year-old from this city, was studying at the Catholic Church. At about 8:00 p.m. last night, he went to the willow tree beside the iron fence of the train station to peek at the summer movie theater. He was spotted by the two-station police, who used a rattan cane to drive him away. Shi Afang panicked and fell from the tree, causing the sharp tip of an iron bar on the iron fence to stab his left lower abdomen. He fell to the ground, bleeding profusely. Shi was rushed to Guanghua Hospital for treatment by his cart, and his life may be in danger.

Meat Industry Storm May Come to an End: The meat merchants in this city have been on strike because of the slaughterhouse problem for three months. The government has not yet come up with a concrete solution. It is now reported that the meat merchants sent representatives, including Mao Mingdi, to petition the provincial government the other day. Liu Shixin, the secretary-general of the provincial government, received them and agreed to send people to conduct an on-site inspection within three days and plan to build a private slaughterhouse to regulate the market. At the same time, the deadline was extended for two months, and business will continue as usual. The representatives were satisfied and returned.

City Chamber of Commerce Appoints Staff: The staff of the City Merchants' Unification Committee were appointed as follows yesterday: Secretary Wang Shuyun, Document Clerk Sun Shi, Recorder Zhang Ruxiang and Dong Yebai, Registration Section Clerks Lin Yongmin, Cai Juting, and Dong Yuanxia, Registration Section Clerks Shen Huan and Xu Yinguan.

Xuzhou 86

Guerrilla Commander Takes Office and Pacifies the People: Yao Zhidao, the guerrilla commander of Xuzhou, Huaihai, immediately set up a temporary office in Xuzhou after being appointed by General Commander Chiang Kai-shek and issued a proclamation as follows: Proclamation Regarding the Case: It has been received that Commander Chiang of the Army, Navy, and Air Force has issued an appointment certificate from the Liuhe Camp, stating that Yao Zhidao is hereby appointed as the Guerrilla Commander of Xuzhou, Huaihai for the Suppression of Rebels. This certificate, etc. Following this, a temporary office was set up in Xuzhou on the 7th of this month, and the official seals and stamps were put into use. The report has been submitted and distributed. At a time when the military is advancing, it is difficult to guarantee that bandits will not collude with the Communists to cause disturbances in the rear. I, the Commander, have pledged myself to the Party and the country, and Jiangsu Province is also my hometown. Eliminating reactionaries, protecting the territory, and pacifying the people are my responsibilities and cannot be neglected. In addition to sending teams to station in important areas of jurisdiction to strictly prevent disturbances, I will inspect the troops in each district after the deployment is complete, so as to ensure strict discipline, eliminate bandits, consolidate the rear, and ensure the safety of the people. If there are unemployed vagrants, local bullies, or hoodlums who falsely use the name of this headquarters to create rumors or cause trouble, they will be investigated and dealt with once they are reported.

Educational News: Important News

Ministry of Education 87

Measures to Improve Higher Education

No More Provincial Universities to Be Established in Areas Near National Universities: Nanjing, 26th--The Ministry of Education has decided on measures to improve higher education throughout the country by reorganizing provincial universities. (1) The existing provincial universities will be reorganized in accordance with the University Organization Law and Regulations. Those that meet the regulations will be expanded in accordance with local needs. (2) The establishment of universities in the future will be decided by the Ministry. (3) When first established, they will be called colleges, with two departments: arts and sciences. Only those with three or more departments will be called universities. (4) No more provincial universities will be established in areas or near national universities.

Another telegram said that the Ministry of Education has decided to merge Chengdu University, Sichuan University, and Sichuan Normal University into one school, establishing colleges of arts, sciences, law, and education with the existing departments, and adding a medical college in the future.

Central Training Department Reviews Party Ideology Textbooks 88

Ministry of Education Orders All Bookstores to Submit by September 10

The Ministry of Education has received a letter from the Training Department of the Central Executive Committee requesting that all recently reviewed books be sent to the Ministry for review for reference and requesting that all bookstores be ordered to submit all party ideology books that have not been submitted for review by a deadline so that the review can be completed as soon as possible. In addition to sending all books that have already been reviewed to the Central Training Department, the Ministry of Education yesterday also ordered the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to order all bookstores to comply and submit all party ideology textbooks that have not been submitted for review by September 10 of this year for review.

The Thirteenth Session 89

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Agricultural Society Opens in Qingdao; Qingdao Correspondence: The Chinese Agricultural Society held the opening ceremony of its 13th annual meeting at 8:00 AM on the 23rd of this month at the Qingdao National University campus. The Qingdao Municipal Agriculture and Forestry Bureau had made preparations to receive everyone in advance. On that day, more than 80 members and guests arrived. Committee Chairman Xu Xuan presided over the meeting. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded below:

Attendees: The members who registered on the day included Xu Xuan, Chen Zongyi, Zeng Jikuan, Bao Bodu, Shao Weikun, Guan Qianfu, Yang Bangjie, Wang Hengzhi, Wang Jinwu, Liu Yunchou, Hao Qinming, Rao Maosen, Su Yaofeng, Sun Chongxin, Yin Zheding, Han An, Wang Kai, Wu Naican, Wang Lanxin, Sun Wenqing, Zheng Chongshi, Jiang Youcang, Zhou Yaqing, Su Linjiang, Wu Jiazhen, Zhang Haiqiu, Gu Yuxi, She Yizhuo, Jiang Derui, Wang Chengjun, Zhou Jianhou, Shen Deren, Zhou Zhongqi, Ge Jingying, You Xiaobiao, Jin Sixu, Zhang Kai, Zhang Jingxian, Liu Baocheng, Bai Cai, Cheng Jinghao, Sha Fengdao, Wang Weirou, Xu Shangda, Ling Daoyang, Liu Dinggong, Yao Yanqing, Zheng Puyi, etc., totaling 48 people. Guests included Cai Yuanpei, Dean of the University Council; Xu Xuan, representative of the Ministry of Education; Liu Yunchou, representative of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining; Kikuchi Akio, Tanaka Sadaji, Suzuki Kozo, Mimatsu Naoji, and Noguchi Yakichi, representatives of the Japanese Agricultural Society; Wang Xi, representative of the Municipal Government; Han An, Director of the Education Bureau; Mou Junde, Director of the Commodity Inspection Bureau; Yang Zhensheng, President of Qingdao University; Ding Jingchen, Standing Committee Member of the General Chamber of Commerce; journalists from the Press Association, and several dozen others.

Chairman's Address: After the meeting began as scheduled, Chairman Xu Xuan delivered the opening address, stating briefly: "Today is the 13th annual meeting of this society. This society has been established for fifteen years since its founding in the fifth year of the Republic. It has contributed very little to the country and society, and I feel deeply ashamed. When a person reaches the age of fifteen, it is of utmost importance. If they are well-educated at this time, they will surely achieve great things in the future. Otherwise, they will achieve nothing in their lives. As this society is at this stage, our colleagues should make special efforts to maintain it, so that it can grow from childhood to adulthood, and not disappoint the expectations of the people of the country. Currently, all countries in the world are experiencing unemployment problems, especially England and Japan. Examining the reasons, England has always relied on industry and commerce to build the country, neglecting agriculture early on. Once commerce declines and industrial production suffers from oversupply, unemployment increases, leading to political and social unrest that cannot be maintained. Although Japan pays great attention to agriculture, it ultimately cannot compare with industry and commerce. Therefore, cities expand and rural areas decline. Once affected by changes in the global economy, unemployment problems arise. It can be seen that if countries around the world continue to focus solely on industry and commerce and neglect agriculture in the future, the danger will be even greater than today. China's agriculture is declining, and it is even more difficult for industry and commerce to compete with the great powers. (Omission) As for agriculture, it is China's inherent industry and easier to develop. Therefore, in the current situation, we should promote industry and commerce on one hand and develop agriculture on the other. However, to develop agriculture, it is essential to start with science. Examining countries like Germany, the United States, France, and Japan, each has its own characteristics in agricultural science, but our country does not. For example, the teaching materials used in agricultural schools are mostly translated from foreign countries, and there is very little research on our country's agriculture. This is undeniable. I hope that colleagues in this society will conduct special research on our country's agriculture in various categories in the future, and develop an independent agricultural science for China. Then the development and improvement of agriculture can be anticipated." After the Chairman finished speaking, Cai Yuanpei, Liu Yunchou, Wang Xi, Kikuchi Hisao, Yang Zhensheng, Mou Junde, Ling Daoyang, Zeng Jikuan, and others gave speeches in succession. Then, they took a photo and adjourned the meeting.

Public Lectures: At 8:00 AM on the 24th, the society held public academic lectures in the auditorium of Qingdao University. The lecture topics and speakers' names are recorded as follows: (1) Professor Kikuchi Akio, Doctor of Agriculture from Tokyo Imperial University, topic determined, not translated. (2) Professor Tanaka Sadaji, Doctor of Agriculture from Tokyo Imperial University, (Characteristics of Agricultural Land Utilization). (3) Suzuki Kozo, Technician and Doctor of Agriculture from the Livestock Experiment Station of the Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry. (4) Chen Rong, Professor of Agronomy at Nanjing Jinling University (Characteristics of Chinese Woody Plants). (5) Yang Bangjie, Director of the Sericulture Department of Guangdong Zhongkai Agricultural and Engineering School (Two or Three Examples of Using Pure-Line Separation to Improve Guangdong Silkworm Varieties). (6) Hao Qinming, Professor of Agronomy and Forestry at Nanjing Jinling University, topic undetermined. (7) Zeng Jikuan, Professor of Agricultural Science at Guangdong Zhongshan University (A Survey of Afforestation Species in Guangdong).

Annual Meeting Schedule: Registration on the afternoon of August 22nd; opening ceremony at 8:00 AM on the 23rd; report on society affairs at 2:00 PM; academic lectures starting at 8:00 AM on the 24th; discussion of agricultural issues at 2:00 PM; presentation of papers and reports on agricultural progress at 8:00 AM on the 25th; discussion of society affairs and elections at 2:00 PM; sightseeing tour at 8:00 AM on the 26th: 1. News from the Jiangsu Yijiao Office's Universal Education Experimental Zone 91

The joint office for preparing compulsory education in various counties of Jiangsu Province has designated Yonggu Township, Zhenjiang, as a universal education experimental zone, named Zhongleng New Village. Chu Xiongbo has been hired as a design committee member to actively carry out the New Village project. A village meeting was held at Dingmao Elementary School the other day, attended by Township Head Cui Guangfu, neighborhood chiefs, and others. The office staff members Chu Xiongbo and Xie Zeren, Dingmao Elementary School Principal Zhang Xixian, and more than 60 guests and villagers were present. Cui Guangfu chaired the meeting, and Xie Zeren served as the recorder. The chairman reported that the Yijiao office would guide the village's transformation, develop the village's economy, improve the village's organization, and promote the village's culture to make the village a model village, on the one hand, to seek happiness for the villagers, and on the other hand, to provide a reference for counties throughout the province. He asked everyone to work hard together to promote progress. Subsequently, Chu Xiongbo reported that in carrying out the village's project, the focus must first be on the economy, as the saying goes, "educate after becoming rich." There are several aspects to the project: (1) Establishing a farm to test and improve agricultural products; (2) Raising fish; (3) Organizing an irrigation cooperative; (4) New Village autonomy. In terms of cultural projects, such as utilizing natural scenery to develop parks and implementing education for young children and adults, these should also be carried out step by step, with the goal of achieving significant progress within three years. Subsequently, the regulations of the Zhongleng New Village Preparatory Committee were approved, and Cui Guangfu, Zhao Debao, Lu Yueting, Tian Dengxi, Yin Derong, Zhang Xixian, and Xie Zeren were elected as executive committee members on the spot. Then, the executive committee held a meeting, appointed members to draft the executive committee's charter, decided on a plan to repair the Dizang Nunnery as an office, and actively prepared for all matters to proceed.

Wuhan University Builds Water and Electricity Plant 92

Since the National Wuhan University selected the lakeside of East Lake in Wuchang to build a new campus, bids have been submitted one after another for the entire project, such as the liberal arts college, science and engineering college, male and female dormitories, auditorium, and faculty residences, and construction has already started. The main buildings are located on the top and hillside of Luojia Mountain, with a majestic appearance. When completed in the future, it will be very spectacular. The faculty residences are built in the style of new villages, with more than 30 buildings in total. Now that various projects have reached a considerable degree, the university has decided that the most important water and electricity supply should be set up as soon as possible. It has decided to build a large-scale water and electricity plant. The drawings and budget have been finalized by the personnel of the university's engineering college. Letters have been sent to well-known foreign merchants of electrical materials in Shanghai and Hankou, asking manufacturers in various countries for prices. Several black oil engines are needed, as well as several generators and water pumps. The generators can supply power to the two colleges of science and engineering, and also for 3,000 to 4,000 electric lights within the campus area. The water pumps can supply drinking water for 3,000 people. Including the installation of water pipes and electric wires, the total construction cost of water and electricity is estimated to be more than 100,000 yuan. The price estimates from various foreign firms have been arriving at the university one after another, and the best will be selected for purchase soon, with the aim of completing the installation within six months.

This City

Municipal Education Bureau Formulates Moral Education Standards 93

Municipal School Academic Performance Assessment Measures to be Announced Soon

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau believes that there are numerous schools in the city, and there is no unified method for moral education management. While there are many who do well, there are also not a few who are lax. The local environment is complex, and the will of young people is not yet determined. If there are no moral education standards, then each school will govern itself or implement them poorly, which is not a blessing for the young people of society. Director Chen has previously appointed a committee to formulate moral education standards for schools at all levels. It is reported that in compiling the moral education standards, the committee, in addition to following the educational purpose, Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, the spirit of the Three Principles of the People, and educational principles, also pays attention to (1) strictness, (2) suitability for local conditions, (3) concreteness and practicability, and (4) consistency.

In addition, the bureau believes that the methods for assessing the academic performance of students in municipal schools are not uniform. Often, the scores assigned to the same course differ greatly depending on the leniency or strictness of the marker, sometimes differing by one or two semesters. School A believes that a student can graduate, while School B may think that the student cannot pass. Students are directly affected by this, and it is also inconvenient to assess their performance. Therefore, the research section has specially formulated various academic performance assessment methods. All aspects of course marking, promotion, retention, graduation, and failing are subject to review methods, with the aim of being consistent with educational principles and easy to calculate. The entire process is nearing completion and will be announced soon.

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Submission of Timetables 94

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to municipal schools and registered private schools stating: "It has been found that schools are required to submit two copies of the current timetable for each grade at the beginning of each semester for verification. It is now found that elementary schools in this city have already started the new semester. In accordance with academic qualifications, the current timetable for each grade in the current semester should be copied and submitted in duplicate by September 3rd for review. This bureau hereby orders all municipal and registered private elementary schools to comply with this order."

The Latest Projects of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute 95

Recent progress in the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute's projects: (1) Guidance for further education: An average of about 15 people per day, mostly young people from other provinces, who are unfamiliar with the content of Shanghai schools, request detailed guidance. (2) Employment guidance: Mostly for graduates of various schools, those who are successful generally have genuine skills, specialized knowledge, and are willing to start small. (3) Service guidance: The institute publicly investigates service performance, and provides encouragement and advice, using both written and spoken methods. (4) Health guidance: Focuses on avoiding occupational diseases and paying attention to self-cultivation and exercise. Recently, with Dr. Ge Chenghui going to the United States for investigation, Dr. Zeng Liqun has been invited to take over. (5) Job placement: This work is the most complex. An average of 50 to 60 letters and telegrams are received daily, and the number of interviews is more than 30 people. In July and August, about 1,000 people registered, but only about one-tenth were successful. Yesterday, a telegram was received from the Hankou Municipal Government Education Bureau, entrusting the recommendation of specialized talent in rattan work, dyeing and weaving, and handicrafts, each with a monthly salary of 60 yuan. The Jilin Provincial Vocational School sent a telegram requesting the introduction of two professors of clerical studies, who must be proficient in Chinese typing, Chinese shorthand, and official document formats, archival processing, service ethics, and library science, with a monthly salary of 120 yuan. In addition, an agency entrusted the recruitment of two clerks, who should be proficient in documentation, have beautiful calligraphy, a clear mind, and a strong body, with a monthly salary of 30 to 40 yuan. Applicants can first submit the drafts and small regular script samples of the documents they intend to write to the institute for consultation as soon as possible. A school in this city is looking for a female teacher to teach 24 hours per week, with a monthly salary of about 20 yuan, and a female teacher for singing, dancing, and handicrafts, with a monthly salary of 10 yuan. (5) Seeking art friends: Entrusted by a certain society, the institute is seeking two art friends who must be clear in writing and reasoning, have beautiful calligraphy, be meticulous, and be ambitious to pursue further studies. The society will teach them various knowledge and research opportunities at any time, and may provide subsidies. Young men and women who are ambitious to serve and seek to improve themselves, and who wish to become art friends, can go to No. 30 Hualong Road at any time to consult with the institute in person.

The Problem of the Fudan Practical Middle School Principal Resolved 96

The Board of Directors Decides to Invite Chen Wangdao to Cancel His Leave and Return to the School

The problem of the Fudan Practical Middle School Principal has not been resolved for a long time. President Li submitted it to the Board of Directors, and a meeting was convened on the 25th of this month. The attendees included Qian Xinzhi, Fang Jiaobo, Wang Zhengting (representing Jin Wensi), Yu Youren, Jin Wensi, Jiang Ping, and Zhang Tinghao. Director Shao Lizi also sent a telegram expressing his opinion. At that time, Director Qian Xinzhi presided over the meeting. First, Secretary-General Jin Tongyin, entrusted by President Li, reported the facts of the case. Then, Director Zhang Tinghao reported the mediation situation, and then the method of resolution was discussed. All directors advocated inviting the original principal, Chen Wangdao, to cancel his leave and return to the school (acting principal Wang Shihao has already resigned). They also discussed the issues of faculty and staff and rectifying the school spirit this semester. Finally, it was resolved: (1) President Li should return to the school to take charge; (2) All follow-up matters related to the Practical Middle School should be handled properly by Director Chen Wangdao in consultation with President Li. After the meeting adjourned, President Li sent a letter to Director Chen Wangdao, asking him to return to the school to take charge immediately. The two-month dispute was thus concluded.

Yesterday 105

Party, Government, and Military Resolution

Preparing for a Mass Rally to Celebrate the Suppression of Communists and Traitors

Scheduled for the Morning of the 29th at the Public Sports Ground

Various organizations and groups in this city, indignant at the Communist Party's poisoning of Hunan and Hubei, and the massacre of innocent civilians, believe it is necessary to thoroughly eradicate them. At the same time, because the rebel army has collapsed and victories are being achieved in the suppression of rebels, the morale of the entire city is exceptionally high. Therefore, it was decided to hold a mass rally to show the determination to suppress the Communists and celebrate the victory over the rebels. Preparations for this event have already begun. Yesterday, a conference was held among representatives from the Party, government, and military to decide on appropriate measures. Attendees included representatives from Party, government, and military organizations such as Yang Qingyuan, Wu Bokang, Chen Junyi, Huang Guangdou, Qi Xuan, Guo Yongxi, and Li Xilong. After formal introductions, Wu Bokang, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Committee, was elected chairman. The resolutions are as follows: The Shanghai Special City Executive Committee submitted a proposal to hold a "Mass Rally to Celebrate the Suppression of Communists and Traitors." Resolution: Passed. (1) Date: Determined to be August 29th at 9:00 AM (Inform all sectors to gather at 8:00 AM). (2) Location: Public Sports Ground. (3) Issue an order to all district Party branches to instruct all affiliated Party members, schools, and factories to participate. Also, the Citizens' Training Association will send a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, instructing all factories to suspend work for one day, with wages paid as usual. (4) Workers from all factories participating in the rally will receive wages as usual for that day (To be announced jointly by the Citizens' Training Association and the Social Affairs Bureau). (5) Security: The Garrison Headquarters, Public Security Bureau, and the Defense Corps will be responsible. (6) Expenses: The Municipal Party Committee will bear two-thirds, and the Municipal Government will bear one-third. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

Jinliyuan Wharf Case 106

Liu Yunfang and Gan Gelin Meet Three Times

Resolving Key Issues Before Arbitration Negotiations

The dispute between the China Merchants Bureau's Jinliyuan Wharf and the French Jesuit "Sandetang" (Three Virtues Hall) has been handled through diplomatic channels. Director Liu Yunfang of the Foreign Affairs Office in Shanghai and French Consul General Gan Gelin have negotiated twice to change the legal procedures to arbitration. The China Merchants Bureau and Sandetang have each appointed arbitrators and are preparing to make contact. However, during the second negotiation, the French Consul expressed to Director Liu the hope that the China Merchants Bureau would first provide a bank guarantee for timely payment of rent, to facilitate the arbitration process, before the arbitrators from both sides formally engage. Director Liu also considered this request reasonable and relayed it to Cai Ziping, General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, and Secretary-General Xu Xiuzhi, asking them to arrange the bank guarantee for timely payment of rent as soon as possible, so that the arbitrators from both sides could meet soon. The China Merchants Bureau obtained the consent of Sun Hengfu of the Siming Bank to provide the guarantee. Yesterday, the China Merchants Bureau formally negotiated with the Siming Bank and decided to use the Bureau's property rental income in Jiujiang as collateral for the Siming Bank to guarantee the rent payment. Cai, the General Manager, prepared an official letter to the French Consul. To ensure prudence and hoping that the French Consul would mediate, Liu was requested to meet with the French Consul yesterday afternoon and explain the contents of Cai's official letter, asking him to forward it. Liu met with the French Consul and briefly explained the content of the Chinese official letter. The French Consul expressed his satisfaction and said he would be responsible for urging Sandetang to order its arbitrators to start negotiations with the China Merchants Bureau's arbitrators as soon as possible. The French Consul also said that while the will of the priests of Sandetang could not fully represent a response, he believed the outcome would not deviate from the spirit of maintaining the old agreement. Liu further stated to the French Consul that since the bank guarantee for timely payment of rent had been resolved, there was no reason or need to increase the annual rent. The French Consul replied that this point was easy to resolve, and even if there was an increase, the amount would be minimal and not significantly different from the original rent. The content of General Manager Cai's official letter to the French Consul is as follows: "Regarding the dispute between our Bureau and Sandetang regarding the lease, we thank you for your mediation and renewal. Our Bureau has appointed arbitrators, and their names and addresses have been sent to you. Regarding the issue of a bank guarantee for the annual rent, we have agreed with the Shanghai Siming Bank to provide a guarantee that the annual rent will be paid in full on time. We hereby notify you, the Consul General, and ask you to verify and inform Sandetang to begin arbitration immediately." Respectfully, to French Consul General Gan, China Merchants Bureau, General Manager Cai Pei, August 26th, Republic of China, 19th year.

Chen Xizeng Returns to Shanghai Yesterday 107

Firmly Declines the Position of General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau

And Hands Over the Directorship of the Telegraph Bureau

Chen Xizeng, Director of the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, after being appointed by the National Government as General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, considered the China Merchants Bureau's future in the shipping industry to be of great importance and felt that his talent and ability were insufficient, and that he was unprepared. If he were to take office rashly without plans for reorganization, he would feel ashamed of the central government's initial intention. Therefore, after receiving the order, he immediately resigned via telegram and went to the central government to express his difficulties. Subsequently, the National Government's Civil Service Office urged him to take office via telegram, and various central figures earnestly tried to persuade him to stay. However, Chen did not change his intention to resign. It is now reported that Chen went to Nanjing again the day before yesterday to personally submit his resignation to President Tan of the National Government. President Tan still indicated that he was unable to approve it. Chen repeatedly stated that if he were to take office, it would not benefit the future of the China Merchants Bureau, and that he was unwilling to take on the position, requesting that he be allowed to resign. Chen returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. A reporter from the "New Voice" visited him yesterday. According to Chen, he is firm in his resignation as General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau. As for the position of Director of the Telegraph Bureau, the Ministry of Communications has appointed Song Shuqiao to take over. He immediately went to the bureau and notified all important staff members to prepare for the handover. Once the handover is completed, Chen plans to go to the front lines to serve.

Discussions on Holding a National Products Exhibition in Singapore

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce, upon receiving an order from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to hold a national products exhibition in Singapore, has issued separate letters to various national products organizations in the city, as well as the silk and satin industry trade unions, stating, "Singapore is the most commercially prosperous area in the Nanyang Islands, with a large number of overseas Chinese residing there. Holding an exhibition in that port to promote national products is an essential plan. In order to develop our country's foreign trade in silk fabrics, the Ministry has issued orders to various overseas Chinese merchants, asking them to assess the timing and collect domestic silk fabrics within the meeting hall to hold an exhibition. The Singapore Chamber of Commerce has responded, reiterating the decision of Shanghai national products manufacturers to send personnel to prepare for the exhibition, requesting that the Shanghai silk industry compile a register of factory names and addresses, and submit samples of silk products and price lists for the exhibition, or send personnel to promote sales." It is now necessary for the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to verify whether the associations have complied. If preparations are underway in accordance with the previous decision, it is necessary to inform silk weaving manufacturers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang to comply. In addition to instructing the Singapore Chamber of Commerce to convene local overseas Chinese merchants to discuss exhibition methods and report for review, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is hereby instructed to comply, directly contact the Singapore Chamber of Commerce for handling.

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce yesterday instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to approve the letter from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stating that the Embassy in France had reported that the Suez Canal Company had notified them that the Board of Directors had decided to reduce the Canal passage tax from 6.90 French francs to 6.65 French francs from September 1 of this year.
