Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 177

— Haike

Old gentleman (seeing an underage child smoking a cigarette): Child, you should know that at your age, you must not smoke cigarettes, because it is very harmful. If you are willing to throw away this half cigarette, I will give you a dime.

Child (throwing away the cigarette): The cigarette has been thrown away. Where's the money? The old gentleman gave him a dime. Five minutes later, he saw him smoking again. Old gentleman: I told you not to smoke, and I gave you money. Why are you smoking again?

Child: Thank you for the dime. It was just enough to buy me a box of high-quality cigarettes. The taste is much better.

New policeman (arresting a person and seeing the police chief): Sir, a robbery occurred on East Street just now. A leather bag was robbed. It was hard for me to catch one person. Please, sir, give an order.

Police chief: Wow, you are so bold and reckless. How dare you rob on the road in broad daylight?

Policeman: Sir, you are mistaken. He is the person who was robbed.

Police chief: Then what are you arresting him for?

Child A: I am a big man. I can subdue the whole world.

Child B: What are you talking about? Do you think I'm a fool?

Child A: Look, that world map is right under my body. It doesn't move at all.

A Glimpse of Ma Fuxiang Passing Through Wuhu on His Return to the Province 178

— Sent from Wuhu by Xueqian

Chairman of Anhui Province, Mr. Ma Fuxiang, has been residing in the capital for a long time since taking office, without returning to the province. Recently, due to the reorganization of the provincial party headquarters, he had to make a trip back to Anhui to reorganize everything. Coincidentally, Director of the Department of Finance, Sun Shengwu, was in Beijing on the 22nd after contacting the Shanghai banking community for a loan, so they returned to the province together.

Mr. Ma and Mr. Sun took the Jiangxin, a China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ship, that day. The Jiangxin is one of the four first-class ships of China Merchants (the others being Jianghua, Jiang’an, and Jiangshun). The decorations are quite good, and although it is old, its sailing power is not weak. It departed at around 11:00 AM that day and arrived in Wuhu at 2:25 PM. The various agencies in Wuhu had already received telegrams and made preparations. Tang Shaogao, the director of the Municipal Police Bureau, had dispatched over a hundred members of the Special Operations Brigade of the Public Security Bureau to be stationed around the China Merchants’ cargo dock in advance. Twenty additional police officers were also deployed on the dock to maintain order. Before 2:00 PM, Shao Yizhou, the director of the Municipal Preparatory Office, County Magistrate Sun Gongming, and Director Jin, the representative of the Bank of China, had arrived at the port one after another. Police Chief Tang also wore his military uniform and supervised everything with the head of the special operations brigade and the inspectors. At 2:20 PM, the ship was approaching the shore, and the police band on the shore played music loudly. Mr. Ma, his wife, daughter, and Director Sun all stood on the port side of the deck. Mr. Ma leaned on the ship's railing with one hand, wearing a light lake-colored gauze long gown, with his bald head uncovered, and frequently nodded to the shore, while talking to his wife from time to time. Madam Ma wore a white qipao and waved a goose feather fan, with a very leisurely attitude. Director Sun wore a white silk long gown, with glasses framed with tortoise shell, his long hair unkempt, standing on the deck with his hands behind his back, about ten steps away from Mr. Ma. Five or six armed guards stood to the left and right. As the ship approached the dock, they successively returned to their cabins. The heads of the various agencies were the first to board the ship and bowed to Mr. Ma in the large dining room. Mr. Ma returned the greetings one by one and sat in the chairman's seat at the large dining table, inquiring about each of the visitors. Soon, Mr. Li Laosan, a reporter from the Wuhu Wanjiang Daily, and leaders of the Chamber of Commerce came to pay their respects. In total, there were fifty or sixty people. The ship stayed for about two hours before gradually leaving the port amidst the music of the military band. Mr. Ma and Mr. Sun still stood on the deck to return the greetings of those who were seeing them off.

A Word on Bare Feet in Guangzhou 179

— Huang Juncai

In the article "Visiting the Empress of the Sea" in this column on the 15th, it was mentioned that there were three aristocratic and fashionable Western women with natural bare feet, not wearing silk stockings. It was said that this was the most fashionable attire for women in Western countries, which attracted the attention of all Chinese people at the time, and that Shanghai women would soon compete to imitate it. The body and limbs are received from one's parents and are inherently pure and need not be concealed. Moreover, people's hands are often exposed, while their feet are covered with socks. Why is there such unequal treatment of hands and feet? It is speculated that the Western women's intention in not wearing socks is also to show the natural beauty of their feet. Whether this kind of dress is beautiful and hygienic is another question. However, it has been seen in Guangzhou, China, for a long time. Today, the West calls it fashionable, which is somewhat laughable. However, the fashion of not wearing socks in Guangzhou did not originate among the aristocracy, but among maids, which is a slight difference.

Wealthy families in Guangzhou employ two types of maids. Those who are responsible for sweeping and other menial tasks are called "dazha" (general help), while those who specialize in folding quilts and making beds and serving the mistress are called "jinshen" (personal attendants). Those who fill the role of personal attendant mostly come from the "self-combed" class (in Cantonese, women who do not marry are called "self-combed"). They are in their late teens or early twenties, with shapely figures. Their winter clothes are light blue cloth, and their summer clothes are black silk, each costing more than ten yuan. They are tailored to fit the body and are elegant and lovely. However, they do not wear socks throughout the year, and their black satin slippers with felt soles expose their heels. The delicate flesh catches the eye. Their ability to achieve this beauty is due to artifice. Every morning, they use pumice stone to rub their heels smooth, and then apply face powder and a little rouge, like a painter applying colors, matching them appropriately, so they appear clean, white, and bright. They look like lotus roots emerging from the water. The beauty of these natural bare feet is probably not inferior to that of Western women.

The original intention of personal maids not wearing socks is unknown. However, considering that their work is leisurely, it is not due to occupational reasons. They can wear black silk outfits costing more than ten yuan, so they certainly cannot be without a pair of socks costing a few cents. It can be seen that it was not initially a matter of money. However, it has been done for a long time without anyone praising it. Now that Western women imitate it, it attracts the attention of the people of the country. In general, the same dress or hobby is called civilization if it comes from a strong country, but it is called barbarism if it is seen in a weak country. This is often the case, so why is the simple matter of not wearing socks any different?

A Record of the Joint Celebration at Liwa Lida Manor 180

— Huang Jiping

A garden party seems to be a very new term. Recently, various groups in Shanghai, when encountering any anniversary, send invitations to people from all walks of life to visit pre-arranged, relatively elegant places, such as parks, lakes, mountains, or beautiful villages, so that people who have lived in noisy markets for a long time can absorb fresh air and cultivate their minds. This is indeed a very meaningful event.

The Photography Pictorial held a reader's gathering on August 24, and designated "Liwa Lida Manor" (Villa Riro Rita) in western Shanghai as the site of the garden party. I have always been very interested in garden parties, especially "Liwa Lida Manor," which I had never set foot in before, which aroused my curiosity. At about 4:00 PM, I boarded the car and set off. The car passed the Fanhuangdu Station and reached the end of Jessfield Road. After crossing the Suzhou River, we arrived at our destination. We walked through a shady path about a hundred meters long and stepped into the garden gate, turning to rest on the grass by the stream. A total of over two hundred guests arrived one after another. The other hundred were all blond and blue-eyed. They were regular customers. There were very few Chinese visitors. This time, the gathering of men and women can be considered the first time ever.

After we found our seats, we took photos, rowed boats, and chatted, each doing as they pleased. The grass by the river, which was about two acres in size, was filled with guests. I felt that women were the most powerful in this kind of gathering. They wore colorful clothes, revealed kind and pleasant expressions, and emitted bursts of莺声燕语 (pleasant sounds like orioles and swallows), which was indeed a good source for regulating the beautiful life between the two sexes. If the gathering were purely of the same sex, it would definitely be less colorful. At that time, there were also several Western women wearing swimsuits, constantly appearing in our sight. They rowed boats, swam, or lay on the grass, or hugged each other, their postures natural, as if showing off their abundant muscles to others. There were also many well-known people among the guests. Chen Jian, the recently retired director of the Ministry of Education, also strolled in the garden, with a leisurely attitude, presumably also happy to be at the garden party.

The owner of "Liwa Lida Manor" is the Russian Korolev. There are vegetable gardens and ridges all around. There are two open spaces with shallow grass in the garden, where people can play ball. The flowers and trees are luxuriant, and the air is fresh. To the west of the venue is a stream that is not connected to the Suzhou River. The stream is about ten feet deep, and the water is quite clear. It is very comfortable to row a boat or swim in the water. In the middle is a small Western-style house. Every night, Westerners come here to dine or dance. However, the materials are still very simple. This villa is not in the concession, but the entrance is marked with No. I Jessfield Road, which does not match the "No. 1 on the north bank of the Suzhou River" compiled by the Public Security Bureau. This is another evidence of the Municipal Council building roads beyond its boundaries. Although this is a small point, we do not seem to be able to neglect it.

Small Report: Pingbao Newspaper Office in Yuren Lane, Yunnan Road, in order to give preferential treatment to subscribers, in addition to giving away a copy of "Yan Zhihu" or "The Original Face" for each year of subscription, one phonograph and a dozen records will also be given for every hundred subscribers. The first group has already been announced. According to the last two digits of the number of the first special prize of the Wanguo Beichu Society in August, those who have the same last two digits as the number of the subscription form will get a phonograph and a dozen records. The last two digits of the first special prize of this Wanguo Savings Association in August are 83. It has been found that it was won by the Second Battalion of the Huainan Smuggling Suppression Navy. The newspaper has already purchased phonographs and records from Baidai Company to give to subscribers. In addition, the newspaper has recently been greatly improved. Such as Zhao Tieqiao Anecdotes, and Crude Oil Is Expensive, and Jin Chao's various articles are extremely valuable. And the social novel "The First Beauty's Romantic History" written by Shulu Shufang is published in each issue, which is extremely insightful. The method of giving preferential treatment to subscribers is still in effect. A reward will be given once every one hundred subscribers.

News from the Publishing World: Zhang Genong from Dantu has a new social novel called "Love Sea Tide." The content is rich, and there are signatures and prefaces by Jiang Hongjiao, Xu Xingchu, Yao Gengkui, Ma Xiezong, and others from the Shanghai news industry. It is said that each book is priced at four yuan, but a special price of only two yuan is offered, and a copy of Baihua, a love letter in brocade cover written by Zhu Songlu of Yunyang, is also included. The general distribution office is the Daya Bookstore diagonally opposite the south end of the Shenbao Newspaper Office on Wangping Street in this city.

An Analysis of the Recent Political Turmoil in Germany (Middle) 181

— Li Liuceng, sent from Paris

After the incident, the political situation in Berlin suddenly became chaotic. The Social Democratic Party was most satisfied with the final voting results in the parliament, because the motion to revoke the government order proposed by the party was declared established by a vote of 236 to 221. The new tax law issued by the cabinet on the 16th based on the constitution could not take effect as a result. However, since President Hindenburg has given the cabinet full power, the implementation of this new tax is to fill the gap in national expenditure, which the cabinet believes is an urgent matter. Therefore, the same order will be issued again in a different way next week. Based on this, the goal of the majority of members of parliament to avoid the implementation of the new tax has not been achieved. However, in terms of public opinion, these members can not bear any responsibility for the implementation of the new tax, whether it is justified or not. It is most important for political parties to concentrate on gaining public opinion in elections, because the public often hates new taxes.

After examining the final voting results of this parliament, we can know the general situation of the various political parties in Germany today. The majority of 236 votes is composed of the Social Democratic Party, the Communist Party, the Nationalist Party, and the Racialist Party (Racistes). Among these political parties, except for the Racialist Party, which is a reactionary political party, and the Communist Party, which is an active revolutionary party, we will not discuss them for the time being. The Social Democratic Party pays more attention to the parliamentary system and democratic order. As for the Nationalist Party led by Xiao Zhenbo, it is similar to the Italian Fascist Party, and is obsessed with military politics. However, in this turmoil, the failure of the Nationalist Party is the same as that of the cabinet. During the voting, the party was divided into two parts. Twenty-five people did not listen to Xiao Zhenbo's orders and followed Duke Westarp to vote in favor of the government. Therefore, the division of the German Nationalist Party this time is a definite fact. We can predict that the Nationalist Party members of the Westarp and Trevinanus factions will soon gather to form a new right-wing political party. Xiao Zhenbo's actions in this incident are tantamount to building a tomb for his party. His dictatorial ideas will inevitably lead to disintegration. In this parliamentary vote, the party was important and had the possibility of cooperating with the cabinet. Xiao did not know how to use the opportunity to incorporate the party's strength into the cabinet, but instead put forward various unacceptable conditions, resulting in a stalemate. It can also be said that he lacked political skills.

Many people believe that this incident is a major crisis for the German republic, constitution, and parliamentary systems. For ten years, dissolving parliament to seek the development of the political situation is the fourth time. It is a dangerous sign of the parliamentary system that the various political parties cannot stabilize the government and implement a policy that is beneficial to the country. The fact that the Brüning cabinet's prudent reform method for finance is the most important plan for Germany today is an indisputable fact. It is incomprehensible that the various political parties lack political courage and do not want to bear joint responsibility in this necessary reform plan, but instead force the government to abandon its specific plans or even adopt similar dictatorial last resorts.

Warmth in My Heart (263) 182

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 13: Who Unintentionally Sows Fortune and Gains a Diamond Ring; Only This Cause and Effect Sings the Song of the Golden Thread with Intent

That day, the banquet ended very late. Of course, I couldn't go to Hundred Flowers Lane. The next day, when Zuo Shichen arrived at the newspaper office, he found a strange letter among the many letters. It was a small, thin red slip envelope. Below it were written the three words "Name: In detail." Zuo Shichen thought to himself, "Who is inviting me to a brothel again?" Because that kind of envelope is known at a glance as a common item in brothels. They don't need sturdy and elegant envelopes, and writing "Name: In detail" on the outside has also become a habit, similar to writing a "Know" character in the signature place of a guest ticket. Zuo Shichen opened it and saw that it was indeed a guest ticket, from Chan Nong's house in Hundred Flowers Lane. Below it was noted the character "Three," so he knew that it was sent by Chan Nong. The characters were written worse than those of a character-splitting fortune teller, probably by the accountant in their place. On the side of the guest ticket were four other characters, written: "Please come and eat crabs." When Zuo Shichen saw these four characters, he thought of her living by Yangcheng Lake. Every year, her family often sent several large baskets of big crabs to share with her regular customers. Now it was time to hold crabs and admire chrysanthemums. He remembered that one year, there was a painter named Yin who was a guest of Cui Yun. Because he ate Cui Yun's crabs, he wanted to paint a picture of "Frosty Claws" to hang in Cui Yun's dressing room. Cui Yun quickly said no. Hanging a picture of several crabs in the room would make people say she was an old crab. Therefore, Old Master Yin changed the painting to chrysanthemums. I say this is a bit of an elegant person's deep understanding, exchanging crabs for chrysanthemums, like Wang Xizhi exchanging paintings for geese. Now that I think about it, her transition from the Cui Yun era to the Chan Nong era really means becoming an old crab. That day, he finished his daily routine business hurriedly. When he could feel his way to 9 o'clock, he came to Hundred Flowers Lane. Although he heard that business was not very good, it was still an upstairs room, with a side room and a pavilion. However, because there were not many customers who came to chat, the lights were not very bright, so it was inevitably a bit dim. Chan Nong hid in that pavilion, wearing a light blue bamboo cloth vest, making a short velvet cord shirt. She put a rose-purple velvet cord ball in the interlayer of the vest. When she saw Zuo Shichen come in, she half raised her body, welcomed him with a smile, and said, "Why did you come so late? I've been waiting for you for a long time." There was an old woman in the room, who was an old person from the Cui Yun era. Zuo Shichen remembered that she was from Luxu, Wujiang. He secretly thought that people who eat brothel food are just like their warlords. If they don't leave the mountain, they're fine, but when they do, they will naturally summon their old troops, and use their old subordinates. Hearing that someone had come out of the mountain again, they would naturally come to return. Sometimes they would even encourage their old masters to come out of the mountain so that they could manipulate power and profit. This time, Cui Yun came out of the mountain, wouldn't it also be encouraged by them?

Drastic Fluctuations in the Gold Market

Rise and Fall... Exceeded Twenty-Three Taels

Conclusion... Rose Thirteen Taels Two

Entirely Dominated by Air; Yesterday, the 26th, the gold market situation had drastic changes, with signs of a renewed high. There were latent opportunities of ten taels, but the waves were turbulent and the momentum was unstoppable. The total rise and fall of the day was more than twenty-three taels. The psychology of the industry was panic-stricken, because it was dominated by air. The foreign exchange market had already lengthened by one gear, but the domestic market tended to be firm, which was a clear picture of looseness on the surface and tightness underneath. The market was divided in buying and selling, and large firms such as Yuan Xing, Yongzhi, Fengyong, Hengxing, Yu Da, etc., came in and out suddenly. As for the silver price, although it rose, it did not move, so the morning market was stable. Later, the exchange rate was long and turned to a low peak. The firms sold together, once breaking 550 taels. However, Yu Da, Yuan Xing, Yong, etc., flocked to buy, and the exchange rate became superior. In particular, the bank telegrams from Mumbai continued to sell silver, so the market atmosphere became sharp and climbed, soaring more than ten taels. Later, the buying intention of Shi Yuan, Sheng, Yu Da, Heng Xing, Yuan Xing, Yong, etc., was very strong, and the public's confidence was strengthened. The exchange rate was even better, and it had exceeded the 570 tael mark. However, there were floating states, because of the stimulation of buying and selling, and finally it reduced by five or six taels, between sixty-seven taels. The silver bar went back up by one-fourth, and the silver price also increased by three-fourths.

Morning Market Wild Retreat and Advance; The opening price of gold in October was 555 taels and 4 qian, an increase of 1 tael and 8 qian. The firms had all entered. Then, it increased to 58 taels 7 or 8 qian. The first announcement was still flat, at 58 taels 4 qian. It was learned that it was long 25, US dollars half a yuan, Japanese gold reduced by 1.75 points. The domestic market also seemed to be loose. Sumitomo first bought November 7 pence 5625, December 6875. Then, the Wheat Company issued November 5625, and Zhifeng, Yongda, Decheng, Yuanxing, Yong, etc., tended to sell, and the price almost went downhill, falling sharply by 10 taels, and finally reaching 49 taels and 5 qian after 10 o'clock. It returned to two or three taels in a moment. After a while, the large households entered again. In particular, large silver bars had the ability to fall again, so they rushed straight into the sky and rose sharply. It had rushed out of 60 taels. By noon, it had risen by more than 15 taels. It closed at 64 taels and 7 qian, and it was linked for more than ten minutes. It was raised to 67 or 8 taels. The announced price had been changed to 627 taels. Because Japanese gold was less than 1.75 points, it was initially suppressed by about 70 taels, noon was 62 or 3 taels.

Evening Market Ups and Downs Even More; The afternoon opening price was 66 taels and 3 qian, and then it was sold by Zhifeng, Yong, etc., and then it dropped to 64 taels 2 or 3 qian. Suddenly, Yuan Cheng started to buy, and immediately jumped up 5 taels, to 69 taels 3 or 4 qian. Yu Da, Fuchang, etc., sold, and it saw setbacks again. At about 2:30, it finally dropped to 62 taels 6 qian. However, the public's confidence was floating and unsettled, and the price was also weakening. HSBC sold September 7 pence 1875. Later, Youli and Holland sold 7 pence 125. The industry was not idle, and Yuan Cheng, Bingxing, etc., scrambled to buy, adding 5 taels again. At 2:45, it was 67 taels 4 or 5 qian, and it retreated slightly to more than 4 taels. After 3 o'clock, the market's buying sentiment was surging, and the bars were extremely scarce, with very little supply. The public's confidence turned strong, and even jumped out of the 70 tael mark. At 4 o'clock, it reached 72 taels and 5 qian. However, the bulls took the opportunity to sell, and it was suppressed by as many as five or six taels. At the close of the market at 4:30, it was 566 taels and 8 qian, compared to the previous day, it rose by 13 taels and 2 qian, and the future may improve. It was found that the maximum price in one day was 72 taels and 5 qian, and the minimum price was 49 taels and 5 qian, a difference of more than 23 taels. The announced price was calculated from 612 taels to 60 taels, and the account was 76 taels to 65 taels. The water replenishment was 76 taels to 78 taels. The early market price was 55 taels and 6 qian, the noon close was 66 taels, the afternoon was 6 taels and 7 qian, and the closing price was 66 taels.

The Transactions Were Very Chaotic; The transactions of each firm were Zhifengyong, Dade, Cheng Hengxing, Yuda, Yuan Xingyong, Yongfeng and other major firms entered and exited without a fixed pattern. Wanxing and Shunli sold more and bought less. Yuanmaoyong and Yiyu all entered. Fuchang and Chunyuanyong all sold. In the afternoon, Yuancheng, Bingxing, Yuan Chengyong, Yuan Xingyong, etc., all entered. Zhifengyong, Tongtaichang, Fuchang, and Yongfeng sold. Wanxing, Shunli, and Taikangrun sold more and bought less. The Dalian gang sold more than 2,000 bars and bought more than 1,000 bars. The Guangdong gang bought more than they sold, about 2,000 bars.

Yarn and Cotton: Marked Yarn Market Turns Stable 189

Overseas cotton yarn market conditions uniformly trended upward, but local sentiment remained weak, with most holding a bearish outlook. Due to sluggish actual demand, sellers continued to exert pressure, and market sentiment remained soft. However, one manufacturer adopted a rather firm stance, showing no intention of easing up. Therefore, the overall situation remains in a state of consolidation.

Auction Gains, Retail Investors Cover Shorts: In the morning auction market, the opening price rose four qian following the firmness of overseas cotton prices, but later fell due to seller pressure. The final result was a rise of one, two, or three qian. In the afternoon, the price of third-grade yarn was firm, and retail investors covered their shorts, leading to a rise of one, two, or three qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 14,050 bales. Of these, Yiyu bought 950 bales, Shenchang 750 bales, Gongtai 800 bales, Yudda 400 bales, and Heshen, Xiesheng, Yidda, Senkang, Tianlong, Daji, Changji, Maoji, Yunde, Taichang, and Yongchang bought between 300 and 500 bales. Major players still have no intention of resisting short positions. However, if overseas cotton rebounds and does not fall again, local cotton may experience a small upward trend.

Grain: Rice Market Plummets 195

Zhabei: Yesterday, arrivals from various regions were around the 20th of the month, and market sales felt even more sluggish. The decline in prices for Northern "po jing" rice was rampant and had no basis. Top-grade "jing" rice was only between 20.02 and 20.03 yuan, while ordinary "jing" rice barely opened at 19.50 yuan. High-grade "jing" rice fell by about 0.03 yuan, while medium and lower grades had to be reduced by more than 0.5 yuan. At the same time, prices for rice from inland areas uniformly reported declines, making it even more difficult for the local "jing" rice market to stand firm. Due to concerns about continuous sharp declines, buyers and sellers of Dongxin new "jing" rice turned to a wait-and-see attitude, so the decline stabilized slightly, opening at 17.50 yuan, similar to the previous price. Thin rice followed the "jing" rice market and went downstream, with large-scale prices hovering around 20 yuan. New, sharp rice saw an even sharper decline, with high-quality goods being inquired about by retailers at 13.65 yuan, while medium-quality goods were only at 12.80 or 12.90 yuan, a large drop of 0.05 to 0.06 yuan compared to the previous day. Tongbian rice also declined by 0.02 yuan, opening at 18.40 yuan.

South Shanghai: There were few arrivals from the river areas, and sales were also extremely sluggish. Top-grade Changxi "po jing" rice was still being inquired about, but buyers had to significantly reduce their bids, so transactions were unsuccessful. Su and Tong "po jing" rice lacked interest from both urban and rural areas, so the market tended to be quiet. Prices were weak, down by 0.02 or 0.03 yuan, and the situation remained weak. New "jing" rice arrivals were slightly scarce, with prices at 17.50 to 17.00 yuan. The market situation remained soft. The South Shanghai thin "po" market was dull, and prices followed the Northern "jing" rice market and became scarce. New Sanjian rice lacked buying interest, down by a small 0.02 yuan, barely opening at 13.70 or 13.80 yuan. Baiyuan rice was scarce in this area and lacked demand, with an overall weak trend.

Wuxi New "Jing" Rice Has Been on the Market for Three Days 196

Initially Opened at 17.70 Yuan...Yesterday Fell to 14.70 Yuan 197

The Wuxi market turned sharply downward in the past two days. Since the arrival of new "jing" rice, the daily arrivals have been abundant, and the Shanghai market has frequently declined, greatly weakening confidence. New "jing" rice initially opened at 17.70 yuan, but yesterday's market fell to 14.70 yuan, a huge drop of 3 yuan. The official price was only around 19 yuan. Therefore, most buyers and sellers holding "po jing" rice stored in various warehouses were eager to sell, so the "po jing" market also declined by as much as 1.5 yuan in two days. This is a reaction after a large increase.

Marked Flour Short Covering Leads to Further Price Increases 198

Yesterday's flour market saw prices rise across all months after the market opened, especially for the current month, as major bulls absorbed shorts, leading to an even more dramatic price increase. The opening price was 2.585 taels, a sharp increase of 0.01 tael compared to the previous close. Prices for other months increased by several li. The current month's delivery is imminent at the end of the month, and major factories have indicated that they will not release warehouse receipts. Small and medium-sized factories have limited strength and do not have many flour reserves, so they will likely not deliver many warehouse receipts. Therefore, the buying atmosphere is even more intense, with a determination to squeeze shorts. The afternoon market saw prices rise again, and floating shorts quickly rushed to cover. Major shorts were also unable to hold on. If no factory releases flour tomorrow or the day after, prices will likely be squeezed even higher. The closing price for the current month increased by another 0.0175 tael, September increased by 0.01 tael, October and November increased by 0.0075 tael, while December and January saw no change.

Wheat Futures Bulls Gain Momentum 199

After yesterday's wheat market opened, large shorts delivered a large batch of goods, stabilizing sentiment. Small longs sold out as the market went, and the market reversed to weaken. However, the current wheat reserves are mostly of medium quality, which do not meet the standards. The bullish momentum is even stronger, with both recent and distant deliveries being bought up. The afternoon opening saw more improvement, and the closing price for the current month increased by another 0.03 tael, September and November increased by 0.03 tael each, October increased by 0.04 tael, and December and January increased by 0.02 tael each. Spot wheat arrivals and reserves were both low, and factory demand was strong. A total of 5,000 bags of wheat from various regions were offered, and prices rose by another 0.05 to 0.06 tael.

Hardware: White Lead Sheet Shows Signs of Movement After a Long Period of Calm 206

The white lead sheet market has been sluggish for a long time, and the standard price has remained unchanged for a long time. Recently, Tianjin merchants have shown signs of movement, and the military procurement office has suddenly started purchasing in large quantities. Therefore, the volume of transactions is almost comparable to the best-selling items among major hardware products. According to inquiries, over the past two days, a total of 140 barrels have been purchased. The price of No. 2 is estimated at 25 taels per dan, No. 3 and No. 4 are both offered at 24 taels, No. 5 is 22 taels and 7.5 qian, No. 6 is 22 taels and 2.5 qian, No. 7 is 21 taels and 7.5 qian, No. 8 is 22 taels, No. 9 is 22 taels and 2.5 qian, No. 10 is 21 taels, and No. 12 and the thickest varieties are priced at 20 taels per dan. It is said that the most active transactions in recent days have been for No. 2, No. 5, and No. 9, with No. 3 and No. 7 also seeing some activity.

Tinplate Market is Quiet 207

The recent trend for tinplate, whether British or American, has been extremely quiet due to the lack of purchases from buyers. Fortunately, there are few arrivals, and inventories are low, so the standard prices remain firm. 90-pound British goods are estimated at 14 taels, and 100-pound goods are estimated at 15 taels and 5 qian. 90-pound American goods are estimated at 16 taels and 2.5 qian, and 100-pound goods are estimated at 17 taels and 5 qian. It is said that only 400 to 500 boxes were offered yesterday.

Shanghai Market

Business News 230

The Golden Star Necktie Company of Fifth Avenue, West of Shilu, announces that the company was founded by Gu Zhongyi, Hu Weijian, and others. Preparations are now complete, and the opening will be soon. Mr. Gu was originally the factory director of a necktie company, and has a long history of experience in manufacturing neckties. Therefore, the products of this company will surely bring a unique brilliance to the national goods industry. In addition, the company's distribution office and manufacturing plant (422 Baoshan Road, the original site of the Peacock Necktie Company manufacturing plant) both have storefronts and are now open for business.

Maoshun Machinery Firm announces that the Shuanghu Brand newly invented various double-explosion single-explosion power-cold diesel engines, genuine horizontal type, with both large and small horsepower cylinders, are exquisitely constructed, occupy very little space, use very little oil, and are especially simple to operate. They are most suitable for large and small steamships, generators, rice milling machines, irrigation pumps, lifting machines, etc. They have long been adopted in various ports, and are considered a revolutionary force in modern machinery. They are managed by this firm at No. 8, A, Jiangxi Road in this city. All models are in stock and welcome for viewing. Currently, for promotional purposes, the prices are set low.

Taikang Canned Food Company announces that yesterday was the first day of the company's big sale. The storefront was unusually crowded. Various biscuits sold extremely well, such as the crispy egg biscuits at two corners per package, seven packages per dollar, and assorted biscuits and salted biscuits at one corner per package, fourteen packages per dollar. These three types of biscuits sold thousands of packages yesterday. Various fruit jellies, large bottles originally priced at five corners and a half, were reduced to four corners, and medium bottles originally priced at three corners, were reduced to two corners. This is truly a special and affordable benefit for customers.

Theater News 231

The Five Star Film Company announces that the company has been in preparation for two months. Most of the founders have left for other matters. Now, many people well-known in the film industry have joined, and the first drama will soon be officially filmed. The script is currently under discussion, and the selection of talent for the roles in the drama will be especially cautious. At the latest, filming will begin in the first ten days of next month.

Paramount Company on Museum Road announces that the details of the return to the United States of American Rear Admiral Byrd and his Antarctic expedition team have been published in the pictorial weekly of the previous issue of Shenbao. The success of this Antarctic expedition can be said to be a great contribution to science. Although human efforts are resolute and enduring, without the aid of scientific tools, fate will prevail over man, and the lives of Antarctic explorers will be lost. When the expedition team set off, the American Paramount Film Company specially commissioned two photographers to go to Antarctica to film on location. The achievements of these two photographers are no less than those of the explorers, because although the world can hear about the expedition, the organization of the team, the preparation for departure, the experiences of the expedition, and most importantly, the true scenery of Antarctic geography, will be passed on to future generations through moving pictures. As the saying goes, "Seeing is believing." Even if we have seen photos of the expedition in Chinese and foreign newspapers and magazines, photos are not as clear and accurate as moving pictures. Therefore, the importance of the Antarctic expedition film is evident. This film has already been shown in major cities in the United States. It took two years to film, using 150,000 feet of film, which was edited down to 8,000 feet. It is a complete record of the essence of this expedition. The premiere started in New York on August 25, 1929. There were two cargo ships at the time of departure, one large and one small. The large one was dedicated to carrying food, exploration equipment, and explorers. The small one followed behind the cargo ship, intended as a lifeboat. The two ships left New Zealand on December 2 and headed for Antarctica. On December 25, they arrived at the Ross Ice Shelf. On the 28th, they established a camp in Whale Bay, named Little America, as the base for the expedition. This was close to the base established by explorer Amundsen in 1912. Byrd's expedition was equipped with all the modern scientific aids needed for exploration, such as wireless telephones and airplanes. These two were the most important items for explorers in recent years. Therefore, three wireless telephone stations and an airfield were built on the ice floe in Little America. The explorers lived entirely in ice and snow. The geology of the Antarctic continent is made of ice, more than two thousand feet thick, below which is the sea. The coldness of such ice and snow can be imagined. After the explorers arrived at the Ross Ice Shelf, they moved the food from the cargo ship to the camp, and then the cargo ship left the Ross Ice Shelf and sailed outside the ice floe, to the Antarctic Ocean, to avoid being surrounded by hard ice in winter and unable to sail back to shore. The explorer's residence was dug deep in the snow, and the walls were tightly covered with thick cloth. The main camp was divided into two, with a tunnel 600 feet long in the middle. Food boxes were piled on both sides of the tunnel. At this time, the Antarctic weather was in summer, with sunlight for 24 hours a day, but the cold was still below 20 degrees below freezing. On January 27, 1929, Rear Admiral Byrd took a large airplane for the first time to observe various places. To the southeast of Little America, he discovered a mountain range and named it the Rockefeller Mountains, to commemorate the oil king Rockefeller, as Rockefeller was one of the enthusiastic donors to this expedition. After April, the winter climate of Antarctica gradually approached, and it was dark for 24 hours a day. The explorers prepared to enjoy the life of this harsh winter. The wireless telephone station built in the base often communicated with the New York radio station. This Little America, separated by more than two thousand miles from human civilization, relied entirely on wireless telephones to avoid becoming a stateless land. The winter in Antarctica is the hottest summer in New York. The temperature in New York is 96 degrees, while in Antarctica it is 72 degrees below freezing. The difference is 168 degrees, so the southernmost part of the earth is the coldest place. After this six-month-long night, on November 28, a mild spring returned. The expedition team prepared a plan to fly over Antarctica, wiping and oiling the large airplane. Recently, a second airfield was established in Antarctica, in case the airplane had to land while passing over Antarctica, then there must be an airfield for the airplane to land. The precision of the preparation is admirable. On the 29th, Rear Admiral Byrd and his large airplane flew around Antarctica, and placed an American flag from the airplane. At this time, Rear Admiral Byrd used the wireless telephone installed in the large airplane to broadcast the news of flying over Antarctica. In an instant, all countries in the world celebrated this unprecedented great Antarctic expedition. As for the actual situation and scenery of the expedition, when this film arrives in Shanghai, it will naturally open our eyes, and so on.

Italian Poetry 233

— Yi Kang

Italian literature in recent years has made more significant leaps than before, because after several years of political calm, the national vitality has recovered, and writers have been able to work in peace. Although their literary works, apart from D'Annunzio and Pirandello, have received little attention, the rise of young writers has greatly increased recently.

In Italian literature, poetry is the most representative of the Italian spirit. Since the Dawn Movement of 1915, poets have worked hard to create following the D'Annunzranism of the patriotic poet D'Annunzio, and have achieved great results. However, after the European War, the inspiration that poets gained from abroad decreased, and the production volume greatly decreased. Recently, there has been a new need for poetry in Italy. A young Milanese editor has begun printing "Collection of Italian Poetry."

The first volume, belonging to Aldo Palazzeschi's poems, has been published. Although he is not a new poet, among the poets who rose after D'Annunzio, he is considered the one who can best maintain the inherent form and style. Because of his friendship with F. T. Marinetti, he was initially a Futurist, but he is actually a writer with a heavy dawn-era mysticism. Reading his time, one can't help but return to the era of twenty years ago, because at that time D'Annunzio was also doing mysterious dreams, so writers of the same era fell into the atmosphere of D'Annunzranism. However, the era of mysticism has passed, and the environment does not allow them to have such dreams. Therefore, during the European War, D'Annunzio abandoned the mysterious life of a poet and went to the front line to fight for the motherland, which completely divided him into two people before and after the war, and also opened up a new era in his life. The second volume, Riccardo Bacchelli, also does not have a new atmosphere. The literary taste is extremely strong, and it is only worth praising for the beautiful impressions and descriptions. The depth of thought is worth leaving a deep impression.

The Italian government, in order to encourage new poets, had previously offered a reward for soliciting a biography of the patriotic poet D'Annunzio. Now, it is vigorously rejecting the mysticism in the literary movement of the dawn period, because mysticism is not suitable for the needs of the new era, and the entire Italian nation no longer needs poets who create art for art's sake. Therefore, the government is trying its best to uplift the Futurists, and trying to use their heroic and vigorous temperament in politics. At the same time, when writers across the country feel that there is no possibility of new literature being produced in Italy, they also agree with the government's efforts. Perhaps the new literature of Italy will be produced in their cooperative cooperation.

Melancholy 234

— Work by the painter Pang Xunqin

D'Annunzio 235

— Yi Kang

Among the existing writers in Italy, the one with the most world renown and the highest status in the country is D'Annunzio, famous for his novels, dramas, poems, and songs. Because he is not only a writer who brags on paper and in his mouth, but he is a practitioner who can actually work for his ideals and sacrifice for his motherland.

During the European War, in addition to the extreme anti-war stance of young literary figures, the old writers in Germany and the Allied countries狂熱were singing enthusiastically for fighting for the motherland and fighting for freedom. However, among the German poet Arno Holz, the playwright Hauptmann, the Belgian poet Verhaeren, the poet Enrle Cammaerts, who wrote "Patriotic Songs," as well as the English Kipling, Shaw, and the French Maurice Barries and Andre Suaies, D'Annunzio can also be considered a writer who practices what he preaches. He abandoned his creative work and joined the air force to engage in aerial warfare, and even flew his plane to the Austrian positions, dropping letters urging the people in Vienna to reflect. After the war, he donated his residence to the motherland as a souvenir of victory. Therefore, in the eyes of the government, D'Annunzio's position is above everyone else.

Among all his works, the most influential to Italian writers is his poetry. His poetry is gorgeous in diction and harmonious in style. After the publication of his poetry collection "Lotus Eaters," he not only became the head of Italian poets, but also immediately became the head of the European literary world. In the so-called Italian dawn period movement, during the years from 1910 to 1915, a group of poets followed D'Annunzio.

In the past few years, due to political instability, there has been no progress in the creation of poetry. Now, because the political situation is stable, and young people also believe that poetry is the only tool to sing and fill Italy, a Milanese editor has begun printing "Collection of Italian Poetry." The viewpoint of collection is not entirely artistic appreciation, but focuses on works that can promote the glory of the Italian nation. In the entire selection, decadent and old-fashioned writers are discarded, and the purpose is to inspire writers and works in Italy that can excite the new era.

Although D'Annunzio is now an established writer, he is extremely supportive of the new Italian youth who come later.

(8) Do not use blue ink for illustrations in the article, and do not use colored paper. Use white paper and black silk drawings.

Social News

Siberia Buries a Large Batch of Imperial Russian Treasures 237

Worth 30 Million Yuan Daily Japanese Iwamoto Wants to Make a Fortune

Tokyo News: Japanese Iwamoto, 67 years old, will depart for eastern Siberia at the end of this month to search for gold, jewelry, etc., worth 30 million daily yen, hidden by former Russian Emperor Nicholas. According to Iwamoto, this treasure was buried by the emperor's adjutant a few weeks before Nicholas was killed in 1917. It was originally worth 100 million daily yen, but part of it was taken away by General Kolchak's subordinates. Iwamoto first heard about this matter from a Korean in January 1928. The Korean heard it from a Russian-Japanese soldier. Iwamoto then told important figures such as the late Okura man, but they did not believe it at first. Iwamoto then went to Korea in May of that year to investigate in detail and learned that it was true. However, entering Russian territory to excavate the treasure would definitely be shot by the Russian authorities, so it has been delayed until now. Now Iwamoto knows the exact location of the burial, and has recently sent personnel to the Russian border. He is also determined to go and work together to find a way to excavate it.

The Danger of the Leaning Tower of Pisa 238

The Leaning Tower of Pisa in Italy is one of the wonders of the world, and is also famous in the history of science, because in the sixteenth century, the scientist Galileo once conducted experiments on it to prove that objects fall from a height at the same speed. Over the years, tourists have flocked to Pisa, and all have marveled at the wonder. But now news has come that the tower is almost in danger.

According to the investigation by the committee of the government in charge of the tower, from 1919 to 1929, the tower's tilt increased by ten millimeters, that is, it must tilt more than one-third of an inch per year. The tower is 180 inches high, and it was already tilted 16 feet when it was completed. If it tilts one foot more, the center point cannot be maintained, and it will collapse like the Leifeng Pagoda in our country. According to the current situation, the tower will not be able to be maintained within three hundred years. What is even more feared is that the increase in tilt will be in geometric progression, not arithmetic progression. If so, the life of the tower will be even shorter. Therefore, those in charge are making every effort to preserve this unique wonder for the world.

After careful investigation by scientists, the reason for the increase in the tower's tilt is mostly due to the ground's inability to support it. According to the calculation of the tower's weight, each square centimeter must bear 10 kilograms of weight, but in recent years, due to the increase in houses next to the tower, it has increased to 11 kilograms, resulting in an inability to support it and gradually sinking. Recently, the four sides of the tower have almost become ditches, and children can float toys in them. The only way to save it at present is to glue the soil next to and under the tower with cement, which may help in case of emergency. This plan has been tested, and the results are very satisfactory. Once the funds are available, construction will probably begin. (Junshan)

Book and Newspaper Introductions

Collection of Folk Rhymes and Proverbs of Wujin 239

— Zeng Yang

Compiled by Wu Shouzhen

To truly concentrate on studying folk art, one must of course quietly find many ways that can evoke the purpose of exploration. For example, when we study "children's rhymes" or "folk songs," it is advisable to collect "children's rhymes" or "folk songs" from various places, gather them together, and conduct a systematic comparative study. We can see what the lives of women in a certain place are like, and we can also see what the customs and customs of a certain place are like. When we discover absolute differences or sudden similarities, we can unconsciously evoke various strong interests. Then, for the study of this literature, we can also obtain the most beautiful and full harvest. This is inevitable. No matter what kind of literature you study, if you work hard in a stereotyped and stagnant way, you will never be able to achieve satisfactory results.

I recently discovered this "Collection of Folk Rhymes and Proverbs of Wujin," which really aroused my unusual joy, because after reading so many so-called folk "songs" and "stories," now reading this thin "proverb," although it only has thirty-odd proverbs, I deeply feel that it has a unique flavor. It's like we eat too many delicious cocoa mandarins, and put an olive with astringency in our mouths to chew it, which is even more refreshing. This is really human nature. I had such a feeling when I read this collection of "rhymes and proverbs."

"Rhymes and proverbs" actually occupy an important position in folk literature. This "rhymes and proverbs" comes from the mouths of the people, and is more meaningful than those created by literati and scholars, because it is completely the expression of true feelings and the manifestation of nakedness. The meanings contained in them are mostly derived from experience, as described in this preface:

"Rhymes and proverbs are not only a very precious folk literature, but also the sound of a social mind of an era or a place. In other words, what rhymes and proverbs contain is not only artistic elements, but also religion, science, morality, habits, education, etc., can be found everywhere, because its creation is not by a poet singing in the deep mountains and valleys, or related to the door, but is accumulated with the experience and human feelings of the public, that is, what individuals want to sing in their hearts and tongues.

The above passage really describes the formation and value of "rhymes and proverbs" extremely thoroughly and precisely. It cannot be denied that "rhymes and proverbs" contain profound implications and upward words. When we open this "Collection of Folk Rhymes and Proverbs of Wujin" compiled by Mr. Wu and read it, we can deeply believe it. It turns out that proverbs are the crystallization of human experience. It is "not baptized by science, so it cannot be regarded as scientific principles, but part of human experience, often because there is no opportunity to organize into science, so it is preserved by relying on proverbs alone. Although proverbs are not as good as science, they are also a valuable part of human experience." Because of this, collecting proverbs is as important as collecting folk songs.

Here, it is divided into two collections. The first collection is "Songs," with a total of 30-odd songs. The second collection is proverbs, with three types: one about the state of the world and human feelings, two about celestial phenomena, and three about climate. Each one is also divided into many small categories, so that we can know at a glance what the proverb refers to. It can be seen that the compiler has put a lot of effort into it.

Sitting and eating will empty the mountains,

If you don't grind, you won't be able to become an adult,

Hair is tied out, strength is squeezed out,

There are only lazy people, no lazy land,

Pigs sleep to grow meat, people sleep to tear down houses,

A dull knife is sharpened on a stone, a dull person is sharpened in the world,

Eat all the bitterness, to be a superior person,

Save on eating, save on using, save on asking for help, three years of rotten rice to buy a cow,

If you cherish food, you will have food to eat, if you cherish clothes, you will have clothes to wear,

Wearing clothes depends on your family, eating depends on where you come from,

It is better to buy expensive things to use, than to buy cheap things to eat,

Eating is not poor, wearing is not poor, if you don't calculate, you will be poor for a lifetime,

In each of these words and sentences, there are thorns piercing our entire hearts, promoting the diligence, thrift, and upward development of a national character with a simple style. Such maxims of warning the world are really impossible to find in books. Even if you can find them, they are not so fluent in words and sentences, and you can sing them naturally, arousing endless interest. Here, is the determination of the value of folk literature. When we read this collection of "proverbs," it is obviously different from when we praise "folk songs." Many of them can indeed be used as models for the words and deeds of today's people. Its content is based on direct experience, so it has been left to modern times, and can still affect the current society. For this reason, I will quote another one below,

People fight for a breath, people are old but their hearts are not old,

Rather die than surrender,

Strong grandfather and grandmother, better than ancestors,

Poor but not discouraged, rich but not crazy,

Bricks and tiles also have a chance to turn over,

Rather starve to death, than be a thief,

If you have ambition, don't be afraid of old age, if you have no ambition, you will grow a hundred years in vain,

Don't count the road when you go out,

People look high, water looks low,

Good horses don't eat the grass they turn back to,

Rabbits don't eat the grass near their home,

This proverb says that a person must have a heroic ambition, strive to create oneself, and have an upward and enterprising mind, running on the right track of all mankind, and there will be unlimited hope in the future. These are all encouraging maxims. We must not ignore them and read them unconsciously.

This collection of "Folk Rhymes and Proverbs of Wujin" is also suitable as a teaching material for primary schools, because it is all the promotion of the experience of the predecessors, and can be used as a reference for primary school teachers who teach Chinese. With this teaching method to guide children, I believe that we will definitely receive benefits beyond people's expectations. Many of the "songs" collected here are heroic and upward, and are rarely seen beautiful songs. Then, this is a good children's book. I hope that enthusiastic primary school teachers will pay attention to it.

Automobile News

Commentary

Mechanized Parking Garage 243

— Ping Bao Yuan

Can Solve Shanghai's Traffic Management Problems

The problem of traffic management is one of the important and difficult issues that modern cities pay attention to. Take Shanghai as an example, the streets are narrow and the number of vehicles is increasing every day. Therefore, those in charge of municipal administration attach great importance to this matter. As for the biggest reason for the accumulation of traffic, it is the parking of cars. Residents are also gradually realizing that they should no longer adopt the policy of parking cars freely anywhere. It is imperative to adopt other ingenious methods of parking.

Therefore, how to solve this major and difficult problem is extremely important. Looking at the city of New York, it has now used scientific methods. The Gander Auto Parking Company, the initiator of the Gander mechanical car advancing method, is currently building a Gander auto parking facility that can accommodate 1,000 cars.

At the Gander Mechanized Parking Garage, you can get a receipt for your car on the lowest floor. The ground floor is exclusively for the needs of the cashier. The area it occupies is wide and has a very high ceiling, without columns to hinder the convenience of entry and exit. When you drive to the elevator door, you can lock the car and get out. Then a manager will send you a retrieval check. When you need the car, just move to the cashier's office and present the check. At the same time, the telegraph machine notifies the elevator operator with a mark. The car will be delivered to the lowest floor within two minutes.

At the Gander Auto Parking Garage, purely with Gander electric parking equipment, combining rapid self-leveling elevators, everything is managed. The so-called electric parking equipment is a standard measure of lightweight rubber towing wheels. When in use, it is placed under the car and the gears are connected to the rubber interconnection. Using four-sided levers, it can be moved forward, backward, up, and down at will. Therefore, the manager does not need to leave his original position at the foot of the elevator and can receive, park, and deliver all vehicles.

Features and Advantages of Auto Parking

(1) Saves Time. The entry and exit of vehicles is more convenient than previous methods. Customers can pick up and drop off their cars on the lowest floor. All cars in the garage are placed by electric parking equipment.

(2) Saves Land. The same size area can store more cars with this method. Tall buildings can accommodate many cars. It is also suitable for smaller and more expensive land. This is very convenient for commercial theaters, hotels, and other areas.

(3) Prevents Damage - "At the Gander Mechanized Parking Garage, no hand will touch your car." Electric parking equipment manages vehicles and also avoids the drawbacks of stains and grease. The speeding of locomotives, excessive use of automatic machines and batteries, and misuse of wheels and brakes, etc., can all be eliminated. Vehicles are parked in steel rooms and drive straight - without curves or minor injuries.

(4) Prevents Theft. Whether it is the customer, the original owner, or the driver, no one is allowed to step into the storage area. Car doors and machine doors can also be locked at will.

(5) Lower Pricing. (A) Lower for commercial use because this type of auto parking garage requires skilled and experienced employees, so fewer people are used. (B) Based on storage location, the capital cost is also cheaper. Mechanized parking garages can instantly park vehicles in tall buildings. Therefore, even in expensive areas, the rent for car parking spaces must not be high.

Gander Mechanized Parking Garage in New York 244

Nash Car Wins Championship in French Competition 245

— Pei Gan

Nash cars participated in the annual French car competition this time. “Your de France” won two championships. One is a gold badge, awarding its perfect and reliable driving. More than 150 people participated in the competition. The other is the famous George Ham Cup, won for high-speed driving on Mount Reims. Both winning cars were Nash 400s, overwhelming the crowd. It is not easy to win this grand prize in an international auto competition.

Two people from Nash participated in the competition. One was Mr. Rowan driving a double-ignition six-cylinder car, and the other was Mr. Dume driving a double-ignition eight-cylinder car. Mr. Dume had won the French road championship. The route taken by the competitors was extremely difficult, but the success of the two Nash cars has its own advantages.

The annual "Tour de France" is the most interesting and moving of the world's auto competitions. In the eyes of European car drivers, this kind of competition combines romantic and mechanical competitions, quite reminiscent of the old Gelatin travels. The public has a national auto exhibition. The old Pike's Peak auto climb and the annual Indianapolis Speedway competition are speed time trials on the Reims Speedway. The double-ignition eight-cylinder car driven by Dume averaged 100 kilometers per hour. The car that won this year's George Ham Cup reached 138 kilometers per hour. Nash cars are easy to drive and move beautifully, and are very safe at high speeds. All these advantages are related to the competition.

The interest of the competition is that all those who participate in the above-mentioned competitions participate in this meeting, and experts judge the pros and cons of various cars. This year's competition started from the Podo Meru in Paris. The entire course has 500 kilometers of rugged roads, totaling eight days of travel. The first encounters are the two places of Điện Harvey and Lire. This competition also includes mountain climbing, which takes place in the mountains of southern France. There are also cold Matto braking and other competitions. The race in Reims is only about speed.

Throughout the course, each station managing the competition has a commissioner in charge. Every morning and evening, they inspect the condition of the cars participating in the competition and evaluate the performance of the cars along the way. Even the smallest shortcomings, such as engine overheating when climbing mountains, malfunctioning pistons, slow turns, and unstable driving, are not ignored by experts. All kinds of shortcomings that drivers inevitably have are subject to strict criticism.

Wherever the car passes, it is parked and exhibited at the management site for the observation of local car drivers. This auto travel competition is called the "Spring Auto Travel Exhibition." Every day, tens of millions of enthusiastic auto competition enthusiasts watch and judge its merits along the way. The auto exhibition held in the Grand Palace of Paris is even more lively. Nash cars have gained special records due to various excellences. They have made many new friends in France. Many specially appointed distributors in the cities and towns that the competition team passed through are also a clear proof of Nash's popularity.

Mr. Rowan, who drove the Nash car in the competition, his double-ignition six-cylinder car was newly shipped from the factory. The double-ignition eight-cylinder car that won the new record was taken from the showroom. The car body and mechanical parts of both cars are standard equipment.

Newspaper experts participating in this travel competition said, "During the difficult journey, the Nash car did not encounter any accidents. The smooth performance is commendable. In Bristol, during the cold Matto development, a Nash car traveled 10 kilometers in five seconds, and it was after a cold rainy night. As for the convenience of driving and the comfort of the springs, Nash is worthy of being the ideal travel car."

Trivial Road Administration News from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi 246

— Wu Fei

Jiangsu Province (1) Since the recruitment of workers to build roads began last December, more than 20 counties have started construction. It is now planned to add a branch road from the South Station to Ganlu Temple to facilitate the transportation of goods between the north and south of the Yangtze River. The construction cost is estimated to be 450,000 yuan, which will be borrowed by the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce and repaid by the Railway Bureau. The Railway Bureau has ordered the Engineering Department to formulate detailed plans and conduct surveys. (3) The Jingwu Highway starts from Andermen in southern Beijing, passes through Jiangning Town, enters Anhui Province, and reaches Wuhu, with a total distance of more than 70 miles. The survey is currently underway, and the construction of the roadbed is being promoted simultaneously. The earthwork project of the first section past Jiangning Town has also started last month. (4) The road from Nanjing to Molingguan is currently being surveyed. Construction will begin as soon as the survey is completed. (5) The stone road surface of the Jinghang Road Jingju section has been completed. There are many cars coming and going. In order to maintain the road surface and manage traffic, a road maintenance office has been set up to take charge of the matter.

Zhejiang Province (1) The Hangzhou-Changxing and Hangzhou-Changhua roads actively built by the Zhejiang Highway Bureau. The roadbed project of the Hangzhou-Changhua road has been completed from Hualong to Yuqian. The mountain opening project will be completed. From Yuqian to Changhua, the earthwork has been completed by 80,000 cubic feet. The water pipe project from Yuqian to Hualongdong can be completed this month. The bridge project has also been completed by 50-60%. The survey between Changhua Yulingguan was also completed last month. Only the road funds are insufficient, and construction has not yet started. The Hangzhou-Changxing road line has been completed, and only the two stations of Shijiaqiao and Yangjiabu have not been completed. (2) The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau is strictly levying the highway, which has a great relationship with Zhejiang's transportation. Engineer Yu Zhewen led a team to survey and determine the route. The route from Yanzhou to Huizhou passes through Fuyang, Xindeng, Fenshui, Jiande, and Chun'an counties. The road is about 300 miles long and more than two-thirds have been built. (3) The Yin-Feng line is planned to start from Yuanzhen Bridge, pass through Qiaoshang Shuichi, Yangjia Wangjia Bridge Dongqiao Tou, and reach Yinjiang Bridge. A station will be added in the middle at Shagang Kou Gongjia. The estimated route length is about 16 miles, and the construction cost is estimated at 50,000 yuan. The local gentry of Yinjiang Bridge will raise the money first. There is also an original Qixiang Bridge in Shangshui. It is now planned to rebuild the railway, and the cost is about 7,000 taels. The local gentry Zhang Shenzhi and others are responsible for raising funds in Shanghai. (4) Zhejiang Province has stipulated the construction of Xiaochang, Jinyong, and Jinpu three light railways. Xiaochang is the first phase, Jinyong is the second phase, and Jinpu is the third phase, which will be carried out in sequence. As for its starting and ending points, the Xiaochang line starts from the Xixing Jiangbian in Hangzhou, which is transported by water, and passes through Xiaoshan, Zhuji, Yiwu, Jinhua, Lanxi, Tangxi, Longyou, and Qu County to reach Changshan, which is 315 kilometers long. In the future, it is also planned to extend to Yushan, Jiangxi, which will increase by 36 kilometers. The Jinyong line starts from Jinhua and connects to the Xiaochang line, passing through Wuyi, Yongkang, Jinyun, and Yongjia, which is 180 kilometers long. The Jinpu line starts from Jinyun and connects to the Jinyong line, passing through Lishui and Longquan to Pucheng in Fujian, which is 178 kilometers long. The earthwork of the first section of the Xiaochang Road has been completed by more than 160,000 cubic meters. The bridge contracting fee for this section is more than 110,000 yuan. According to the contract, it must be completed within three months. Construction started on the 7th and 8th of last month at Xiaochang Xinzha Bridge, including Daqiao Panjia Bridge and other places. The earthwork of the second section has been completed by 120,000 cubic meters. The bridge must be completed within three months as stipulated.

New Aishan Keshui's New-Style Table Version 247

Jiangxi Province The main highways of Jiangxi Province are now divided into five categories: (A) Gan-Yue Line, starting from Nanchang, passing through Fengcheng, Qingjiang, Xingan, Xiajiang, Jishui, Ji'an, Xingyuan, Ganxian, Nankang, Dashou and other counties, with a total length of 1,000 li. (B) Gan-Xiang starts from Xinyun, passing through Nanchang, Gao'an, Shanggao, Wanzai, Ping County and other counties, with a total length of 500 li. (C) Gan-Zhe Line starts from Nanchang, passing through Jinxian, Dongxiang, Yuping, Yujiang, Guixi, Yiyang, Qianshan, Shangrao, Yushan and other counties, with a total length of 500 li. (D) Gan-E Line starts from Nanchang to Anyi, Zhanggongdu, and Baicha, with a total length of 460 li. (E) Gan-Min Line starts from Liangjiadu on the Gan-Zhe Line, passing through Nanchang, Linchuan, Nancheng and other counties, with a total length of 440 li. From this, it can be seen that after the completion of the main highways in Jiangxi Province, the transportation with neighboring provinces will definitely be convenient. In addition, there are two lines from Jingde to Hukou and Jiujiang to Lushan, with a total length of more than 270 li. The total length of the line is more than 3,000 li, and the required funds are about 10 million yuan. It is now being built in three phases. The Gan-Yue, Gan-Zhe, Gan-Xiang, Jing-Hu, and Jiu-Lu lines are the first phase. The Gan-Min and Gan-E lines are the second phase. The construction of permanent bridges in various counties is the third phase. The work is carried out separately. The only ones that have been built are the Nan-Zhang section of the Gan-Yue Line, with a total length of 180 li.

Shanghai-Taicang Auto Company Installs New Road Signs 248

— Xin

The Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Auto Company operates between Shanghai and the Liuhe Town and Jiading in Taicang County. The business has been increasingly developed in recent days. It is expected that the vehicles are running on time and the scale is neat. Recently, in order to facilitate passengers and recognize the route, the company specially ordered craftsmen to rush to make a large number of road signs (the same as trams). It is installed on the front of the car. The black background and white characters are very clear. It is said that each one costs about eleven or twelve yuan. There are Shanghai, Dachang, Gujia Town, Liuhang, Luodian, Liuhe, Xinjingqiao, Jiading, and other places and fixed car styles. This move is of great benefit to passengers. It can avoid the trouble of searching. Other stations can also be seen from a distance before the car arrives. It has now been installed and is half completed. It is said that it will be completed soon.

News of the Arrival of the Latest Road Building Machine in China 249

In recent years, transportation undertakings in various places have been developing rapidly, and especially in the southern provinces of the Yangtze River, there are the most builders of new roads. However, they are all due to the huge projects and the lack of good machinery, which leads to prolonged delays and increased costs. The German merchant Lihe Foreign Company in this city, in view of this, will bring the latest trenching and road building machine from overseas to Shanghai. The front of the machine is a silkworm-type car. The front and rear wheels are connected to extremely wide toothed chain. It crawls on the ground, just like a silkworm moving, so it can climb mountains and descend slopes, and it can also walk on loose ground. There is a motor, which is 30 horsepower. Its work is to dig ditches and dig mud on one side, and at the same time use the dug mud to build a fish-back-shaped road. Division of labor and cooperation, it is done in one go. Working 10 to 12 hours a day, it can build 3 miles of road, which is about 9 Chinese miles. The daily consumption cost, such as fuel and machine

Page 28

Oil and all other expenses included, at most, it does not exceed 30 yuan. In this way, a hundred miles project will take no more than ten days. The cost is less than 400 yuan, and it can be completed and opened to traffic. Compared with the current artificial excavation, the time and cost are far from comparable. It is said that Lihe Foreign Company, in order to demonstrate the function of the machine, plans to wait for the machine to arrive in Shanghai and submit a request to the Municipal Works Bureau to allow it to conduct on-site experiments. At that time, the engineer of the company will point out everything. The company especially welcomes people from all walks of life who are concerned about road administration to visit.

Miscellaneous

Small Experiences in Renting Cars 250

— Ping Xin

In Shanghai, the traffic is extremely congested. Not to mention that pedestrians are in fear, even those who sit in cars are afraid that the driver will cause trouble in the middle of the road, and they often break out in a cold sweat. When I first arrived in Shanghai, I liked to rent very beautiful cars. The drivers were all energetic, and when they drove, they rammed all the way, showing off their skills. At that time, I seemed to have rushed into the enemy's defense line on the battlefield. It was extremely dangerous. I couldn't wait to jump out of the car immediately and say to the driver, friend, let me down. I can't stand this kind of shock.

Recently, I rented a sedan, it seems to be a Ford. The situation is different. His driver drives very cautiously. I can determine that he has undergone strict training. It is said that there is also a kind of machinery installed on their cars to limit the rate, so that passengers can be more courageous and at ease.

Because of the above-mentioned small experience in renting cars, I feel that the first thing to pay attention to when renting a car is the safety issue. As for the style of the car, the 1930 style is good, and the 1929 style is also good. This brand is good, and that brand is good. It doesn't matter. Because no matter how beautiful the car is, the notice is always white with black characters. Who doesn't know it's a rental car?

The new Buick car is envied and praised by everyone. This is one of the certificates.
